    12. Hom mpempem hom akoko wɔ mfuwa fɛɛfɛw no ntsi, wɔ wenyindua a ɔsow wosowoso no ntsi.
    13. Nsoɛ na nkɔkrɔw befifir me man asaase no do; nyew, wɔ enyigye kurow no mu enyigye adan nyinara do mpo:
    14. na wɔbɛdan ahemfi no egya; kurow a nyimpa bitsibitsi wɔ mu no bɛda pan; koko no na aweɔmfo aban no bɛdan etu ara daa, na ɔbɛyɛ sar do nsoasopɔnkɔ enyigyebea, na mbowakuw edzidzibea;
    15. dze ekesi dɛ wobefi sor ehue sunsum no egu hɛn do, ma sar no adan asaaseber a ɔma ndɔbaa, na woebu asaaseber a ɔma ndɔbaa no dɛ kwaa.
    16. Ɔno na atsɛmbu bɛtsena sar do, na ndzeyɛtsenenee atsena nsaaseber a ɔma ndɔbaa mu.
    17. Na ndzeyɛtsenenee bɔsow asomdwee aba; na ndzeyɛtsenenee no nsunsuando ayɛ kommyɛ na awerɛhyɛmu daa.
    18. Na me man bɛtsena asomdwee tsenabea, na efiefi a osi pi, na ahomgye mbea komm mu.
    19. Na ɔsorbo bogu wɔ kwaa n'asehwe mu; na wɔbɛbrɛ kurow no adze koraa.
    20. Esiarfo nye hom a hom pe aba wɔ esu nyina ho, na hom to ɔnantwi na asoaso anan kwan.

    Tsir 33

    1. Due, ɔwo ɔsɛɛfo a ɔwo dze, wɔnnsɛɛ wo bi; na ɔkontompɔnyi a wonntwaa wo nkontompɔ bi! Ber a egyaa dɛ esɛɛ no, wɔbɛsɛɛ wo bi; na ber a ama nkontompɔtwa abɔ adze no, wobotwa wo nkontompɔ.
    2. Ao EWURADZE, yɛ adom ma hɛn; ɔwo na hɛn enyi da wo kwan: ɔwo yɛ hɛn abasa adzekyee nyina, hɛn nkwagye so wɔ ɔfona ber mu.
    3. Weɔɔweɔɔyɛ ne dede ntsi na aman eguanguan; w'ahomado ntsi na amanaman apetse.
    4. Na wɔbɔboa hom asadze ano dɛ mbrɛ esa boaboa ano; dɛ mbrɛ mbɛbɛw tutu na wobotutu esi do.
    5. Wɔakrɔn EWURADZE; osiandɛ ɔtse sor noho: ɔdze atsɛmbu nye tsenenee ahyɛ Zion ma.
    6. Na ɔbɛyɛ wo ber mu amandwee, nkwagye, nyansa, na nyimdzee mbordo: EWURADZE ho suro nye n'akoradze.
    7. Hwɛ, hɔn akatakyi retsea mu wɔ guado: asomdwee ho ahembɔfo rusu osu wen.
    8. Akwantsempɔn atɔ pan, ɔkwantsemfo egyaa mu twa: wɔato ahyɛmu no, woebu adasefo enyimtsia, wommbu ɔdasanyi bi.
    9. Asaase no dzi nkɔmbɔ, ɔfɔn: Lebanon enyi ato na oetwintwam koraa: Saron ayɛ dɛ sar pradada; na Bashan na Karmel popo hɔn haban.
    10. Afei na mobɔsoɛr, EWURADZE na ɔse; afei na mebɛma moho do; afei na wobohuhor me.
    11. Hom benyinsen ntsɛw, na hom awo mburonan: hom ahom yɛ ogya a ɔbɛhyew hom.
    12. Na aman bɛyɛ dɛ kaadow nhyewee: dɛ nsoɛ a woetwa a wɔhyew wɔ ogya mu.
    13. Hom a hom wɔ ekyirekyir, hom ntsie dza mayɛ; na hom a hom bɛn, hom ngye mo tum nto mu.
    14. Zion mu ndzebɔnyɛfo akoma etutu; ahohim afa hɔn a wonnyi Nyankopɔn mprase. Hɛn mu woana na ɔnye ogya a ɔhyew bɛtsena? Hɛn mu woana na ɔnye daa nhyewee no bɛtsena?
    15. Nyia ɔnantsew ndzeyɛtsenenee mu, na ɔkasa tɔɔtsen mu; nyia okyir apempensi ho mfaso, ɔpopo ne nsa ho wɔ mboabadzi ne ka ho, osisiw n'aso wɔ abɔgyasɛm ne tsie ho, na omuamua n'enyi wɔ bɔn no hwɛ ho.
    16. Ɔno na ɔbɛtsena ɔsorsor: no twitwagyebea bɛyɛ abotan aban: obenya n'edziban; no nsu nnkɔbɔ no.
    17. W'enyiwa bohu ɔhen no wɔ n'ahoɔfɛw mu: wɔbɔhwɛ asaase a ɔtrɛ kɔ ekyirekyir.
    18. W'akoma bɔdwendwen ehudze no ho: nyia ɔkan no wɔ hen, nyia oker ntoboa no wɔ hen? Nyia ɔkaan abantsentsen no wɔ hen?
    19. Innkohu ɔman yerɛyerɛw no, ɔman a hɔn kasaa mu dɔ a innkotum ehu mu no; apɔtɔfo a innkotum atse hɔn ase no.
    20. Hwɛ Zion, hɛn afahyɛ kurow no: w'enyiwa bohu Jerusalɛm, tsenabea komm no, ntamadan a orunntutu, wɔronnhohɔr no mbɔfodua no ara pɛn, no ho ahoma so mu biara renntsetsew.
    21. Na hɔ na EWURADZE nye hɛn bɛtsena tumdzi mu, esutsen atɛtɛr na nwora bea; hɔ na ntabon ahɛn biara nnkɔkɔ, na ahɛn akɛse so nnkotwa mu wɔ hɔ.
    22. Na EWURADZE nye hɛn tsɛmbuafo, EWURADZE nye hɛn mbrahyɛfo, EWURADZE nye hɛn hen; ɔbɛgye hɛn nkwa.
    23. Wo ntampehoma mu agogow; woenntum ennsusuo hɛndua no ase dzen, woenntum anntserɛw abradaa no mu: ɔno na wɔbɛkyekyɛɛ asadze kɛse a wɔfae no mu; mpakye mpo na bɛfa afomdze.
    24. Na ɔmamfo no mu bi nnkɛse dɛ, Meyar: na wɔdze ɔman a wɔtse mu no hɔn emumuyɛ bɛkyɛ hɔn.

    Tsir 34

    1. Amanaman e, hom ntwe mbɛn mbetsie; na aman e, hom nyɛ aso: wɔmma asaase nye ne mayɛ ntsie; wiadze, nye ndzɛmba nyinara a wofi mu ba.
    2. Na EWURADZE wɔ ebufuhyew wɔ amanaman nyinara do, na ebufuw wɔ hɔn dɔm nyinara do: ɔasɛɛ hɔn huntuhuntu, oeyi hɔn ama okum.
    3. Hɔn atɔfoe so wɔbɔtow hɔn egu, na hɔn efun no bɔnee bɔfow sor, na wɔdze hɔn bɔgyaa anan mbepɔw.
    4. Na ɔsor dɔm nyinara wɔbɛnan, na wɔabobɔw ɔsorsor dɛ nwoma: na hɔn dɔm nyinara bɔpo egu, dɛ mbrɛ ahaban fi wenyindua do po, na dɛ mbrɛ adɔmbadua do haban ɔpo.
    5. Na m'afona anom amee wɔ ɔsor: hwɛ, obesian aba ebobu atsɛn wɔ Edom, na ɔman a madom no no do.
    6. EWURADZE afona ho ayɛ bɔgya ma, wɔdze seradze asera ho, wɔdze nguambaa nye nguannyin bɔgyaa, na nguannyin nsɛbɛ ho seradze. EWURADZE wɔ ɔhyew afɔr wɔ Bozra, na okum kɛse wɔ Edom asaase do.
    7. Na anantwi abɔyafo dze hɔn bɔhwehwe famu, na anantwisaa ɔnye anantwinyin so. Na bɔgya bɔbow asaase, na seradze ayɛ huntuma sɔɔsɔɔ.
    8. Na ɔyɛ EWURADZE n'awerdzi da, nhyɛananmu afe a obedzi ama Zion.
    9. Na no nwora bɛdan ihua, na no huntuma adan ogya sɔɔfee na n'asaase adan ihua a ɔdzɛw.
    10. Worunndum no adzesaa anaa adzekyee; no wusiw bɔfow sor daapem: ɔbɛyɛ amamfo ofitsi ebusuasantsen akɛpem ebusuasantsen; na obiara nnkotwa mu dabiarada.
    11. Na akoroma na kɔtɔkɔ na wɔbɛfa; na patu na akonkoran atsena hɔ; na ɔdze asakrabutuw ahoma, na amamfoyɛ promo bɛsa do.
    12. Wɔbɛfrɛ no, Ahenmanhun a obiara nnyi mu, na ne mbapɔmba nyinara nnkɛsɛ hwee.
    13. Na nsoɛ befifir n'ahemfie, nsason na nkɔkrɔw wɔ n'akoban mu: na ɔbɛyɛ mpataku tsenabea, nsohor adampan.
    14. Na mbowa abɔyafo na mpataku behyia wɔ hɔ, na apɔnkyenyin bɛka mu afrɛ ne nyɛnko; nyew, hɔ anadwe sunsum bɔn bɛtsena, na oenya ahomgyebea.
    15. Hɔ na patu bɛyɛ no buw, na ɔatow, na oesuow mba, na ɔaka hɔn aboa ano wɔ no nwinwin ase: nyew, hɔ na nsansaa bɔboa hɔn ano, obiara nye ne tsiafo.
    16. Hom nhwehwɛ EWURADZE nwoma no mu, na hom nkenkan. Iyinom mu biara nnkɛyew, obiara ne tsiafo nnkɔbɔ no: na EWURADZE n'ano na ɔahyɛ, na no sunsum na ɔapra hɔn aboa ano.
    17. Na ɔatwe hɔn ho tonto, na ne nsa na ɔdze susuhoma akyekyɛ mu ama hɔn: wobenya ayɛ hɔndze daa, na wɔatsena mu fitsi mbasantsen do ekodu mbasantsen do.

    Tsir 35

    1. Sar do na asaase kɛsɛɛ do bɛyɛ enyigye; na sar pradada edzi ehurusi, na ɔahan dɛ nhyiren huanhuam.
    2. Ɔbɛhanhan mbordo ara, na ɔdze dɛw na adwontow mpo edzi ehurusi; wɔdze Lebanon enyimnyam Karmel na Saron abɔsoyɛ no bɛma no: wobohu EWURADZE n'enyimnyam, hɛn Nyankopɔn n'abɔsoyɛ no.
    3. Hom nhyɛ nsa a ɔayɛ mberɛw no dzen, na hom mmiamia anankoroma a egura no mu.
    4. Hom nse hɔn a hɔn akoma etu no dɛ, Hom nhyɛ dzen, mma hom nnsuro! Hom nhwɛ, hom Nyankopɔn dze awerdzi, nye Nyankopɔn ne nhyɛananmu bɛba; ɔbɛba abɛgye hom nkwa.
    5. Ɔno na enyifurafo enyiwa bobuebue, na etsitsifo asowa mu ebuebue.
    6. Nna ebubua bohuruhuruw dɛ ɔtwe, na omum ne tɛkyerɛma atow ndwom: na esuesu botuetue wɔ sar do, na nwora wɔ sar pradada do.
    7. Na anhwea hyehyeehyew no bɛdan nsutaae, na asaase kwawee no adan mbansu: mbrɛ nkyɛ mpataku butubutuwii no, nkyɛkyɛr befifir hɔ aka ndzɛmbir na mbɛw ho.
    8. Na ɔtsempɔn bɛda hɔ, na wɔbɛfrɛ no Krɔnkrɔn kwan; ɔhoɔfifo nnkɛfa do; na ɔno na wɔdze bɛma hɔn: na nkwasea mpo, wɔnnkɔfom kwan wɔ mu.
    9. Ogyata biara nnkɛba hɔ, eso abowa dzifodzepɛfo biara nnkɔfow afa do, wonnkohu hɔn wɔ hɔ; na hɔn a wɔapon hɔn no na wɔbɛnantsew hɔ.
    10. Hɔn a EWURADZE agye hɔn no, wɔbɛsan aba, na wɔdze adwontow aba Zion; na daa enyigye bɛtsena hɔn etsifi: wobenya ahomka na dɛw, na awerɛhow na nkrumsi eguan akɔ.

    Tsir 36

    1. Afei ɔbaa dɛ ɔhen Hezekia n'afe a otsia duanan no mu no, nna Asiriahen Senakerib fowee baa Juda nkurow a wɔagyegye ho ban nyinara do, na ɔbɛgyee.
    2. Na Asiriahen somaa Rabsake ma ofi Lakis dze dɔm kɛse baa ɔhen Hezekia nkyɛn wɔ Jerusalɛm. Na obegyinaa etsifi nsutaae a ɔwɔ ɔtanhofo haban ne tsempɔn no do suka no ho.
    3. Nna Hilkia ba Eliakim a ɔhwɛ fidua no do no, na ɔkyerɛwfo Sebna, na Asaf ne ba ɔsɛnkaafo Joa, fiir edzi baa ne nkyɛn.
    4. Na Rabsake no see hɔn dɛ, Afei hom nka nkyerɛ Hezekia dɛ, Mbrɛ ɔhen kɛse, Asiriahen no, ɔse nye yi, Awerɛhyɛmu bɛn nye yi a edze wo werɛ hyɛ mu yi?
    5. Meka dɛ, w'egyinatu na w'ahoɔdzen wɔ ɔsa ho no, ɔyɛ nsɛnhun kwa: afei woana na etwer no, ma atsew mo do etua yi?
    6. Hwɛ, ɔwo etwer ndzɛmbir a ebu yi no poma do, mekyerɛ Egypt do a; ɔno no do na sɛ nyimpa biara twer a, ɔwɔ ne nsamu, na ohwira mu: mbrɛ Egypthen Farao tse dze ma hɔn a wɔtwer no do nyinara nye no., #Eze 29.6
    7. Na sɛ ese me dɛ, Yɛtwer EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn a: ana nnyɛ ɔno na Hezekia eyiyi ne mbea sorɔnsorɔm na n'afɔrmbukyia, na ɔase Juda na Jerusalɛm dɛ, Afɔrmbukyia yi enyim na hom nsɔr no?
    8. Dɛm ntsi afei, meserɛ wo, enye mo wura Asiriahen no nkyiakyia, na memma wo mpɔnkɔ mpemebien, kyerɛ dɛ w'afamu ibotum ama nyimpa atsenatsena hɔn do.
    9. Na ibodua dɛn koraa etum adan mo wura no nkowaa nketseaba mu ɔsafohen baako n'enyi, ma osian atseaseanam na mpɔnkɔdofo ntsi edze woho akɔtwer Egypt yi?
    10. Ana afei mekwetsir EWURADZE na maba asaase yi do dɛ merebɛsɛɛ no? EWURADZE na ɔsee me dɛ, Fow kɔ asaase yi do, na kɛsɛɛ no.
    11. Nna Eliakim na Sebna na Joa see Rabsake dɛ, Meserɛ wo, kasa kyerɛ wo nkowaa wɔ Siria kasa mu; na yɛtse, na mma nnye hɛn nnkasa wɔ Judafo kasaa mu wɔ nkorɔfo a wɔwɔ ɔfasu no do no asomu.
    12. Na Rabsake see dɛ, Ana mo wura asoma me dɛ membɛka nsɛm yi nkyerɛ wo wura, na ɔwo a? Ana nnyɛ nkorɔfo a wɔtsetse ɔfasu do no nkyɛn na wɔasoma me, dɛ wɔnye hom ndzi hɔnankasa hɔn egyanan, na wɔnye hom nnom hɔnankasa hɔn dwansee?
    13. Nna Rabsake gyinae na ɔdze ndze kɛse tseaa mu wɔ Judafo kasaa mu, na ɔsee dɛ, Hom ntsie ɔhen kɛse no, Asiriahen no, ne nsɛm.
    14. Mbrɛ ɔhen se nye yi, Mma hom mma Hezekia ndaadaa hom; na orunntum nngye hom:
    15. Nkyii so mma hom mma Hezekia mma hom nntwer EWURADZE, dɛ, Ɔgye ara na EWURADZE bɛgye hɛn; wɔremmfa kurow yi nnhyɛ Asiriahen nsa.
    16. Mma hom nntsie Hezekia: na mbrɛ Asiriahen se nye yi, Hom nye me nsiesie na hom mfir edzi mbra me nkyɛn; na hom mu obiara ndzidzi no wenyindua do, na obiara n'adɔmbadua do bi na hom mu obiara nnom nankasa no supi mu nsu:
    17. nkodu dɛ mebɛba mabɛfa hom akɔ asaase a ɔtse dɛ homankasa hom asaase yi do, eburow na wenyin asaase, edziban na wenyin nture asaase.
    18. Hom nhwɛ yie ma Hezekia anndɔkɔdɔkɔw hom, dɛ, EWURADZE bɛgye hɛn. Ana amanaman enyame efi Asiriahen ne nsamu pɛn?
    19. Hamat na Arpad enyame no wɔwɔ henfa? Sefarvaim enyame no wɔwɔ henfa? Aso wɔagye Samaria efi me nsamu a?
    20. Amanaman yi mu enyame nyinara mu woana mu na wɔagye hɔn asaase efi me nsamu, ma EWURADZE rebɛgye Jerusalɛm efi me nsamu yi?
    21. Na wɔkaa hɔn ano too mu, na woemmbua no asɛm biara: osiandɛ ɔhen no ne mbrasɛm nye dɛ, Mma hom mmbua no.
    22. Nna Hilkia ne ba Eliakim a ɔhwɛ fidua no do no, na ɔkyerɛwfo Sebna, na Asaf ba ɔsɛnkaafo Joa, dze hɔn ntar a wɔatsetsew mu baa Hezekia nkyɛn, na wɔkaa Rabsake ne nsɛm no kyerɛɛ no.

    Tsir 37

    1. Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a ɔhen Hezekia tsee no, ɔtsetseew ne ntar mu, na ɔdze eyitam kataa noho, na ɔkɔr EWURADZE ne fie.
    2. Na ɔsomaa Eliakim a ɔhwɛ fidua no do no, na ɔkyerɛwfo Sebna, na asɔfo no mu mpanyin, wɔdze eyitam akata hɔn do, ma wɔkɔr Amoz ne ba nkɔnhyɛnyi Isaia nkyɛn.
    3. Na wɔsee no dɛ, Mbrɛ Hezekia se nye yi, Ndɛ da yi ɔyɛ ɔfona, na nkaenyim, na ɔsesar da: osiandɛ mba edu awoko mu, na ahoɔdzen nnyi hɔ a wɔdze bɔwo hɔn.
    4. Annyɛ a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛtse Rabsake a no wura Asiriahen asoma no dɛ ɔmbɔsopa tseasefo Nyankopɔn no, ne nsɛm no nyinara, na ɔaka n'enyim wɔ nsɛm a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn atse no ntsi: dɛm ntsi ma wo mpaabɔ do ma nkaa no a wɔaka no.
    5. Nna ɔhen Hezekia no nkowaa no baa Isaia nkyɛn.
    6. Na Isaia see hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ hom nkɛka nkyerɛ hom wura nye yi, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Mma nnsuro nsɛm a atse no a Asiriahen no nkowaa dze aka mo ho ebususɛm no.
    7. Hwɛ, medze sunsum bi mebɛhyɛ no mu, na ɔbɛtse huhu bi, na ɔasan akɔ nankasa n'asaase do; na mebɛma ɔatɔ wɔ afona ano wɔ nankasa n'asaase do.
    8. Nna Rabsake sanee na okohun dɛ Asiriahen reyɛ Libna do sa: osiandɛ ɔatse dɛ oetu efi Lakis.
    9. Na ɔtsee dɛ wɔreka wɔ Etiopiahen Tirhaka ho dɛ, Oefir edzi dɛ ɔnye wo robɔko. Na aber a ɔtsee no, ɔsomaa abɔfo ma wɔkɔr Hezekia nkyɛn, dɛ, ISA.37.10, Mbrɛ hom nkɛka nkyerɛ Judahen Hezekia nye yi, dɛ, Mma mma wo Nyankopɔn a edze wo werɛ twer no no ndaadaa wo, dɛ, Wɔremmfa Jerusalɛm nnhyɛ Asiriahen nsa.
    10. Hwɛ, ɔwoara atse dza Asiria ahemfo dze ayɛ asaase nyinara, dɛ wɔasɛɛ hɔn pasapasa: na ɔwo na wɔbɛgye wo nkwa anaa?
    11. Ana amanaman a m'egyanom asɛɛ hɔn no hɔn enyame no egya hɔn, dɛ Gozan, na Haran, na Rezef, na Edenmba a wɔwɔ Telasar no?
    12. Henfa na Hamathen na Arpadhen, na Sefarvaim kurow, na Hena, na Ivahen no wɔ?
    13. Na Hezekia gyee nwoma no wɔ abɔfo no nsamu, na ɔkenkanee: na Hezekia sii mu kɔr EWURADZE fie, na ɔkɛtserɛw mu wɔ EWURADZE enyim.
    14. Na Hezekia bɔɔ mpaa wɔ EWURADZE enyim, see dɛ, ISA.37.16, Dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn a etse kerubfo do, ɔwo wankotoo ara nye asaase do ahenman nyinara do Nyankopɔn, ɔwo na ayɛ ɔsor na asaase.
    15. EWURADZE e, brɛ w'aso adze, na tsie; EWURADZE e, bue w'enyiwa, na hwɛ: na tsie Senakerib ne nsɛm a ɔdze asoma dɛ wɔmfa mbɔsopa tseasefo Nyankopɔn no.
    16. Ampaara, ao EWURADZE, Asiria ahemfo asɛɛ amanaman na hɔn asaase, ISA.37.19, na wɔatotow hɔn enyame egu ogya mu: osiandɛ wɔnnyɛ enyame, na nyimpa nsaano edwuma a, dua na ɔbo; dɛm ntsi na wɔasɛɛ hɔn.
    17. Dɛm ntsi afei, hɛn EWURADZE Nyankopɔn e, gye hɛn fi ne nsamu, ma asaase do ahenman nyinara nhu dɛ ɔwo nye EWURADZE, mekyerɛ ɔwoara nkotsee korɛ.
    18. Nna Amoz ne ba Isaia somaa ma wɔkɔr Hezekia hɔ, dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se nye yi, Susuampa dɛ abɔ mpaa etsia Asiriahen Senakerib no, ISA.37.22, iyi nye nsɛm a EWURADZE aka wɔ no ho: Ɔbaabun Zion babaa no, oebu wo enyimtsia na oesi wo atwetwe; Jerusalɛm babaa no a, ɔawosow ne tsir wɔ wo do.
    19. Woana na asopa no aka no ho ebususɛm yi? Na woana do na ama wo ndze do etsia, na ama w'enyiwa atratra wo ntɔn wɔ no do yi? Nsɛ edze etsia Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no bi a?
    20. Ɔwo nam w'abɔfoe do asopa EWURADZE, na ase dɛ, Medze me ntseaseanam dodow na mobɔfow maba mbepɔw etsifi, akɔ Lebanon mu noho noho ara; na mubotwitwa ne nkyindur atsentsen, na ne pepeaa a wɔapa no egu: na makɛhɛn n'etsifi too, ne habanber kwaa no mu.
    21. Emi na metutu mbura na manom nsu, na medze m'ananadze mobɔwew Egypt esutsen no nyinara.
    22. Ana enntsee dɛ mahyehyɛ no dadaada, na mifi tsetseberdo na mehyehyɛe? Afei na mama aba mu, dɛ ɔwo ebɛsɛɛ nkurow a wɔagyegye ho ban, ma wɔadandan ekurofo ekuwekuw.
    23. Ɔnam dɛ ekuromfo no hɔn tum suar ntsi, hɔn akoma tui na hɔn enyim guu ase; wɔtse dɛ haban mu efuw, dɛ eburow kwa a onnyae nnyinii.
    24. Naaso emi, minyim w'asetsena, wo mfiredzi na wo mbamu, na wo dam a ebɔ wɔ mo do no.
    25. Osian wo dam a ebɔ wɔ mo do, na w'enyimenamsɛm a afow ebodu m'asomu ntsi, medze mo nkwaba mebɛhyɛ wo hwen mu, na medze me menyiamfrɛ ato w'anomu, na mebɛsan wo ekyir afa ɔkwan a enam do bae no do akɔ.
    26. Na iyi bɛyɛ wo asɛnkyerɛdze; afe yi mu hom bedzi dza noara efifir, na afe a otsia ebien no mu dza obefir noara mu epue; na afe a otsia ebiasa mu no hom ndua, na wombu, na wɔntsetsɛw wenyin nture, na wondzi no mu aba.
    27. Na Juda ofi mu nkaa a woefi nsa no wɔbɛgye ndwow akɔ famu bio, na wɔasow aba akɔ sor.
    28. Na Jerusalɛm na nkaase bi befir edzi efi, na hɔn a wobefi nsa so efi bepɔw Zion do: dɔm EWURADZE ho mbɔdzembɔ na ɔbɛyɛ yi.
    29. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE ka wɔ Asiriahen ho nye yi, Ɔremmba kurow yi mu, na ɔronntow hɔ egyen menaba so, nkyii so ɔremmfa kyɛm mmba n'enyim, eso ɔronnhɔr pempe wɔ do.
    30. Ɔkwan a ɔnam do bae no, ɔnoara so na ɔnam do bɛsan akɔ, na ɔremmba kurow yi mu, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    31. Na mebɛper kurow yi magye no nkwa, wɔ mankasa me ntsi, na m'akowaa David ntsi.
    32. Na EWURADZE no bɔfoe fiir edzi kokunkum Asiriafo nserabando nyimpa mpemɔha eduowɔtwe enum: na aber a nyimpa soɛɛr anapaatu no, nna hwɛ, hɔn nyinara adan efun.
    33. Nna Asiriahen Senakerib fii hɔ na osii mu sanee, na ɔkɛtsenaa Ninive.
    34. Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a ɔrosɔr wɔ no bosom Nisrok fie no, nna ne mbabanyin Adrammelek na Sarezer dze afona kum no: na wofii nsa guanee kɔr Ararat asaase do. Na ne babanyin Esar-haddon dzii hen wɔ n'ananmu.

    Tsir 38

    1. Nda no mu no na Hezekia yaar owuyar. Na Amoz ne ba nkɔnhyɛnyi Isaia baa ne nkyɛn, na ɔsee no dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Siesie wo fie yie; na ibowu, na irinnya nkwa.
    2. Nna Hezekia daan n'enyim kɔr ban ho, na ɔbɔɔ mpaa maa EWURADZE, ISA.38.3, na ɔsee dɛ, Ao EWURADZE, mototɔ serɛ wo, afei kaa mbrɛ mesi na manantsew w'enyim wɔ nokwar na akoma a odzi mu mu, na mayɛ dza oye wɔ w'enyi do. Na Hezekia suu yayaayaw.
    3. Nna EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Isaia nkyɛn, dɛ, ISA.38.5, Kɔ, na kɛse Hezekia dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE w'egya David ne Nyankopɔn no se nye yi, matse wo mpaabɔ, mehu wo nyinsuwa: hwɛ, medze mfe duenum mubogu wo nda do.
    4. Na mebɛgye ɔwo na kurow yi mefi Asiriahen nsamu: na mobɔbɔ kurow yi ho ban.
    5. Na iyi nyɛ asɛnkyerɛdze a ofi EWURADZE hɔ mma wo, dɛ EWURADZE bɛyɛ adze a ɔaka yi:
    6. Hwɛ, mebɛma ntwerba no do sunsuma a ewia ama esian wɔ Ahaz n'ewiadɔn do no, ɔasan ekyir ntwerba du. Nna ewia saan ekyir ntwerba du wɔ ewiadɔn a oesian dada no do.
    7. Judahen Hezekia ne nsɛm a ɔyaree na ɔbɔɔ esu fii ne yarba no mu no ɔkyerɛwee nye yi.
    8. Mekaa dɛ, Me nda no wigyinae mu no, mebɛkɛhɛn samanadze aponkɛse no mu: Wɔagye me mfe nkaa wɔ me nsamu.
    9. Mekaa dɛ, Munnkohu EWURADZE, wɔ atseasefo asaase do; Murunnhu nyimpa bio wɔ wiadze mu atsefo no mu.
    10. Wɔama me tsenabea efi hɔ, na woeyi no me nkyɛn kɔ dɛ oguanhwɛfo ntamadan: Mabobɔw mo nkwa dɛ ɔtanwemfo; nkyɛ orubotwa me efi nsadua mu akyen: Da kor adzesaa na ibowie me.
    11. Musui frɛɛ mboa kodur anapa; dɛ ogyata, obubu me mbiew nyinara mu: Da kor adzesaa na ibowie me.
    12. Mokrɔɔw dɛ akyemfowa anaa dɛ nantwinoma; Midzii nkɔmbɔ dɛ ebubur: mohwɛɛ sor ma m'enyi bui; Ao EWURADZE, mo ho akyer me, ɔwoara yɛ me okyirtaafo.
    13. Menka dɛn o? Ɔnoara na ɔaka akyerɛ me, na ɔnoara so na ɔayɛ. Mebɛnantsew berɛberɛ me mfe nyinara wɔ me kra n'ahoguan mu.
    14. EWURADZE, ndzɛmba yinom do na adasa nam tsena ase, Na no mu koraa na mo sunsum no nkwa wɔ: Dɛm ntsi bɔ me esu, na ma minnya nkwa.
    15. Hwɛ, m'asomdwee ntsi na minyaa ahoguan kɛse: Na ɔwo na me kra ho dɔ ntsi eyi no efi mprɔwee amona no mu; Osiandɛ ɔwo atow mo bɔn nyina egu w'ekyir.
    16. Na samanadze runntum nnyi wo ayɛw, owu runntum nntonton wo: Hɔn a wosian kɔ adakamona mu no runntum nnhwɛ wo nokwar no kwan.
    17. Ɔtseasefo, ɔtseasefo, ɔno na obeyi wo ayɛw, dɛ mbrɛ mereyɛ ndɛ da yi: Egya da no nokwar no edzi kyerɛ mba.
    18. EWURADZE ayɛ krado dɛ ɔbɛgye me nkwa: Dɛm ntsi yɛbɔtow mo ndwom wɔ nsankutsen ano Hɛn nkwa nda nyinara wɔ EWURADZE fie.
    19. Afei na Isaia aka dɛ, Wɔmma wɔmfa adɔmba etɔw kor, na wɔmbɔ no boa ntar pɔmpɔ no do, na ɔbɔbɔ esu.
    20. Hezekia so aka dɛ, Asɛnkyerɛdze dɛ mobɔkɔ EWURADZE fie nye bɛn?

    Tsir 39

    1. Aber no mu no, Babilɔnhen, Baladan ne ba Merodak-baladan, somae ma wɔdze nwoma na akyɛdze brɛɛ Hezekia: osiandɛ ɔtsee dɛ ɔyaree, na ɔabɔ esu.
    2. Na Hezekia nyaa ho ahomka, na ɔdze n'adɔnadze dan, dwetɛ, sika, nduhuam, ngo pa, na n'akodze dan, na dza wohunii wɔ n'akoradze bea mu hɔ nyinara kyerɛɛ hɔn: biribiara nnyi ne fie, anaa n'ahenman nyinara mu a Hezekia ammfa annkyerɛ hɔn.
    3. Nna nkɔnhyɛnyi Isaia baa ɔhen Hezekia nkyɛn, na ɔsee no dɛ, Nyimpa yinom bɛkaa dɛn? Na wofi henfa baa wo nkyɛn? Na Hezekia see dɛ, Wofi ekyirekyir asaase do baa me nkyɛn, Babilɔn a.
    4. Nna ɔsee dɛ, Ebɛnadze na woehu wɔ wo fie? Na Hezekia buaa dɛ, Dza ɔwɔ me fie nyinara woehu: biribiara nnyi m'adzekoradze mu a memmfae nnkyerɛɛ hɔn.
    5. Nna Isaia see Hezekia dɛ, Tsie dɔm EWURADZE ne nsɛm.
    6. Hwɛ, nda reba a dza ɔwɔ wo fie nyinara, na dza w'egyanom akora do ebodu ndɛ da yi nyinara wɔbɔsoa akɔ Babilɔn: hweeara rennka, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    7. Na wɔbɛfa wo mba a wobefi wo mu a ebɔwo hɔn no mu binom akɔ, na wɔakɛyɛ asaa wɔ Babilɔnhen n'ahemfie.
    8. Nna Hezekia see Isaia dɛ, EWURADZE asɛm a aka yi, oye. Na ɔkaa no ne tsir mu dɛ, Asomdwee na amandwee bɛba wɔ me nda mu.

    Tsir 40

    1. Hom nkyekye, hom nkyekye me man werɛ, hom Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    2. Hom nkasa akomatɔmu kasa nkyerɛ Jerusalɛm, na hom mpaa mu nkyerɛ no dɛ n'akodzi abɔ adze, wɔdze n'emumuyɛ akyɛ no; dɛ oenya EWURADZE ne nsamu ntsea mbɔho wɔ no bɔn nyinara ntsi.
    3. Obi ne ndze tsea mu dɛ, Hom mbɔ EWURADZE no kwan wɔ sar do, hom ntsen sar pradada do tsempɔn no mma hɛn Nyankopɔn.
    4. Wɔbɛma bɔnsa biara do, na bepɔw na koko biara wɔbɛbrɛ no adze: na wɔatsentsen dza akyeakyea, na mbrɛ ɔyɛ kekakeka no ayɛ dɛfɛɛ:
    5. na wɔbɛda EWURADZE n'enyimnyam edzi, na adasa nyina abɔ mu ehu: na EWURADZE n'ano na ɔaka.
    6. Obi ne ndze ka dɛ, Tsea mu. Na mesee dɛ, Mentsea mu dɛn? Honam nyina yɛ nkyɛkyɛr, na ne fɛw nyina tse dɛ hamu nhyiren:, #Jas 1.10, 11; 1 Pet 1.24
    7. nkyɛkyɛr kyenkyen, nhyiren pa; sɛ EWURADZE n'ahom huw fa do a: ampaara ɔman no yɛ nkyɛkyɛr.
    8. Nkyɛkyɛr kyenkyen, nhyiren pa: naaso hɛn Nyankopɔn n'asɛm dze, obetsim hɔ daa.
    9. Ɔwo a eka nsɛmpa kyerɛ Zion, kɔ bepɔw a ɔkrɔn no do; ɔwo a eka nsɛmpa kyerɛ Jerusalɛm, fa ahoɔdzen ma wo ndze do; ma do, mma nnsuro; se Juda nkurow dɛ, Hom nhwɛ, hom Nyankopɔn nye yi!
    10. Hwɛ, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn bɛba dɛ ɔkatakyi, na ne basa bedzi nyim ama no: hwɛ, n'akatua wɔ ne nkyɛn, na n'ahyɛnanmu wɔ n'enyim.
    11. Ɔbɛnyɛn no nguankuw dɛ oguanhwɛfo, ɔbɔboaboa no nguambaa ano wɔ n'abaw mu, na oetur hɔn no bo mu, na ɔaka nguan a wɔma enumfo berɛberɛ.
    12. Woana na oesusu esuesu wɔ ne nsayamu, na ɔato ɔsor nsatseama, na ɔahyɛ asaase huntuma wɔ etwadze mu, anaa oeker akoko na mbepɔw wɔ nsɛn mu?
    13. Woana na ɔakyerɛ EWURADZE no sunsum kwan, anaa ɔakyerɛkyerɛ no dɛ ɔyɛ ne pamfo?
    14. Woana na ɔnye no tuu egyina, na woana kyerɛkyerɛɛ no, na ɔkyerɛɛ no atsɛmbu kwan mu, na ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ no nyimdzee, na ɔdze ntseasee tsempɔn kyerɛɛ no?
    15. Hwɛ, amanaman tsetse dɛ bokitsi mu nsosɔe, na woebu hɔn dɛ nsɛn mu huntuma ba: hwɛ, ɔmema nsupruw no do dɛ adze ketseaba.
    16. Na Lebanon nnso hyew, no mu mbowadoma so nnso ɔhyew afɔr.
    17. Amanaman nyinara mmfata hwee wɔ n'enyim; wobu hɔn dɛ adze a ɔnnsɛ hwee, na egyangyandze.
    18. Woana ho koraa na hom dze Nyakopɔn bɔto? Anaa suban bɛn na hom dze bosusu no?
    19. Ohonyi a woesian no, odwimfo na ɔnanee, na sikadwinnyi dze sika dura ho, na ogugu ho dwetɛ ntweaban.
    20. Nyia odzi hia dodow no, ɔsan mu yi dua a ɔmmprɔw; ɔhwehwɛ odwimfo nyansafo ma noho, ma ɔaayɛ ohonyi a woesian a onnkotutu.
    21. Aso hom nnhunii? Aso hom nntsee? Aso wommfii ahyɛse nnkaa nnkyerɛɛ hom? Aso hom mmfii asaase ne fapem ase nntsee ase?
    22. Ɔno nye nyia ɔtse asaase no kɔntɔnkrɔn no do, na no mu atsefo tsetse dɛ mbɛbɛw; ɔno a ɔtserɛtserɛw ɔsorsor mu dɛ ɔtam, na ɔtserɛtserɛw mu dɛ ntamadan a wɔtsena mu
    23. ɔno a ɔma mbapɔmba yɛ dɛ wɔnnsɛ hwee; ɔma asaase do atsɛmbuafo yɛ dɛ egyangyandze.
    24. Nyew, wɔnntsetsɛɛw hɔn; nyew, wɔmmfaa hɔn nnduaduae; nyew, hɔn dua nngyee asaase do ndwow: nkyii so ohuw gu hɔn do, na wɔkyenkyen, na ekyinehyia mframa tu hɔn kɔ dɛ ntsɛw.
    25. Woana koraa na hom dze me bɔtoto no ho, ma menye no asɛ? Ɔkrɔnkrɔnnyi no na ɔse.
    26. Hom mma hom enyi do wɔ sor, na hom nhwɛ nyia ɔbɔɔ iyinom, ɔno a obu hɔn dɔm ano dze hɔn pue: ɔbobɔ hɔn nyinara edzin frɛfrɛ hɔn: wɔ n'ahoɔdzen ne kɛseyɛ ntsi, na osiandɛ ɔyɛ dzen wɔ tum mu ntsi, no mu kor ara mpo nnyew mmfi mu.
    27. Afei ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na ɔwo Jakob, eka, na Israel, ekasa, dɛ, Mo kwan ehuntsa EWURADZE, na me Nyankopɔn ebu n'enyi egu m'atsɛmbu do yi?
    28. Aso innhunii? Aso enntsee? Ɔdomankoma Nyankopɔn nye EWURADZE, ɔno a ɔbɔɔ asaase n'ewiei no a, ɔnntɔ bitsi, eso ɔmmberɛ; na ne ntseasee so mu nnyi nhwehwɛmu.
    29. Ɔno na ɔma nyia ɔtɔ bitsi ahoɔdzen; na nyia onnyi ahom no, ɔto n'ahoɔdzen mu.
    30. Mbofra mpo wɔbɔtɔ bitsi na wɔaberɛ, na mberantsɛ ahwehwe ase koraa.
    31. Naaso hɔn a wɔtweɔn EWURADZE dze, wobonu hɔn ahoɔdzen mu fofor; wɔdze ntsaban botu afow sor dɛ nkɔr; wobotu mbirika, na wɔnnkɛberɛ; wɔbɛnantsew, na wɔnnkɔtɔ bitsi.

    Tsir 41

    1. Nsuano aman e, hom nka hom ano nto mu wɔ m'enyim; na aman nnu hɔn ahoɔdzen mu fofor: wɔntwe mbɛn; na wɔnkasa: hom mma yɛmbɔ mu nhyia asɛndzii.
    2. Woana na ɔwosoow obi fi boka no, woana na konyimdzi dzi n'ekyir wɔ beebiara no? Ɔdze amanaman dzi n'enyim, na ɔma odzi ahemfo do tum; ɔdze hɔn ma n'afona dɛ huntuma, dɛ mburonan a wɔbɔ no kɔ ma n'egyen.
    3. Otsiw hɔn, na otwa mu sen sɔnn; wɔ ɔkwan a n'anan nnsii do da mu mpo.
    4. Woana na ɔayɛ na oedzi dɛm dwuma yi, dɛ ɔrefrɛfrɛ mbasantsen fir ahyɛse yi? Emi mara EWURADZE a, ɔkandzifo nye okyidzifo no a, Emi nye no.
    5. Nsuano aman hunii, na wosuroi; asaase ewiei ho popoe: wɔtwee bɛnee, na wɔbae.
    6. Wɔkɔr hɔn ho mboa nkorkor; na obiara kaa kyerɛɛ no nua dɛ, Hyɛ akokodur.
    7. Nna duadwinnyi hyɛɛ sikadwinnyi dzen, na nyia ɔdze hamɛr siesiee ho no yɛɛ nyia ɔbor tombo do dɛmara, ɔreka wɔ ɔsɔw no ho dɛ, Oye: na ɔdze mprɛgow bobɔɔ mu dzen amma oenntutu.
    8. Na ɔwo, Israel, m'akowaa, Jakob a masan mu meyi wo, me nyɛnko Abraham asefo.
    9. Ɔwo a mifi asaase ano noho mesuo wo mu, na mifi ne mfɛndzanan mafrɛ wo aba, na mase wo dɛ, M'akowaa nye wo, masan mu meyi wo na monntoow wo nnkyenee.
    10. Mma nnsuro, na menye wo nam; mma w'akoma nntu, na emi nye wo Nyankopɔn: mebɛhyɛ wo dzen; nyew, mobɔboa wo; nyew, medze me ndzeyɛtsenenee abanyimfa bosuo wo mu egyina.
    11. Hwɛ, hɔn a woenya wo ho ebufuw nyinara bɛfɛr na hɔn enyim egu ase: hɔn a wɔnye wo fimfen nyinara bɛyɛ gyan, na wɔayew.
    12. Ebɔhwehwɛ hɔn, naaso innkohu hɔn, mekyerɛ hɔn a wɔnye wo dzi aper no a: hɔn a wotu wo do ɔsa no bɛyɛ gyan, na wɔasa.
    13. Na emi mara EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn na medze wo nsa nyimfa mu, na mese wo dɛ, Mma nnsuro; mobɔboa wo.
    14. Mma nnsuro, ɔwo abowaba Jakob, na hom Israelmba; mobɔboa wo, EWURADZE na ɔse, na wo pomfo nye Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no.
    15. Hwɛ, mebɛyɛ wo ɔporowdadze fofor ndam ndam a ɔwɔ se pii: ebɔporow mbepɔw na ayam hɔn wekowekoweko, na ayɛ nkoko dɛ ntsɛw.
    16. Ibohuw hɔn, na mframa asoa hɔn akɔ, na ekyinehyia mframa abɔ hɔn apetse: na ɔwo dze ibedzi EWURADZE mu ehurusi, ebɛhyehyɛ woho wɔ Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no mu.
    17. Abɔbɔfo na ehiafo hwehwɛ nsu naaso bi nnyi hɔ, na nsukɔm ntsi, hɔn tɛkyerɛma do wow; emi EWURADZE mara na mubobua hɔn, emi Israel Nyankopɔn mennkɛpa hɔn.
    18. Mubotuetue nsutsen wɔ mpampaa pataa do, na nsunyiwa wɔ mbɔnsa finimfin: mebɛma sar ayɛ nsutaae, na asaase kɛsɛɛ ayɛ nsubaa.
    19. Mebɛtsɛw nkyindur, akeesia, ohuamdua, na ngodua wɔ sar do; medze kupresi na ɔsɛsɛw na ɔpapaa dua bɔbɔ mu esisi sar pradada do:
    20. ama nyimpa aahwɛ, na woeehu, na wɔaadwendwen ho, na wɔaatse ase prɛko, dɛ EWURADZE ne nsa na ɔayɛ iyi, na Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no na ɔabɔ.
    21. Hom mbɛka hom asɛm, EWURADZE na ɔse; hom mbɔ hom nkurow a ɔyɛ dzen biara, Jakob ne Hen na ɔse.
    22. Wɔmma wɔmmbra, na wɔmbɛkyerɛ hɛn dza obesi: hom nda adadadze no edzi, mbrɛ wɔtse, ama yaadwendwen ho, na yeehu hɔn ewiei; anaadɛ hom nkyerɛ hɛn ndzɛmba a ɔreba.
    23. Hom nda ndzɛmba a daakye ɔbɛba edzi ma yenhu dɛ hom yɛ abosom: nyew, hom nyɛ biribi papa, anaa hom nyɛ bɔn, ma hɛn ho mbow hɛn, na yɛmbɔ hu.
    24. Hwɛ, hom fi adze gyangyan mu, na hom ndwuma so yɛ adze gyan: ekyiwadze nye nyia ɔsan mu yi hom.
    25. Mekenyan obi fi kwaamu afamu, na ɔaba; obi a ɔbɔ me dzin fitsi wipuei a: na ɔbɛba ambradofo do dɛ oritsia dɛtse do, na dɛ ɔwemfo ritsia awendɛtse do.
    26. Woana na ɔada no edzi fir ahyɛse, ama yeehu? Ɔnye kankantsetse no, ama yaase dɛ, Ɔyɛ ndzeyɛtseneneenyi? Nyew, obi nnyi hɔ a ɔda no edzi, na obi nnyi hɔ a ɔkyerɛ, nyew, obiara nnyi hɔ a otsie hom nsɛm.
    27. Emi na mibedzi kan mase Zion dɛ, Hwɛ, hwɛ hɔn; na mebɛma Jerusalɛm obi a ɔdze nsɛmpa ba.
    28. Na sɛ mohwɛ a, nyimpa bi nnyi hɔ; hɔn mu ɔpamfo bi nnyi hɔ a, sɛ mibisa hɔn ho asɛm a, obobua me asɛm kor mpo.
    29. Hwɛ, hɔn nyinara yɛ egyangyandze: na hɔn ndwuma yɛ adzehun hɔn ehonyi a woegu no yɛ mframa na enyimguase.

    Tsir 42

    1. Hwɛ m'akowaa a mesuo no mu egyina; me nyia masan mu meyi no a me kra enyi gye no ho: medze mo sunsum ahyɛ no ma; ɔdze atsɛmbu bɛba Amanamamfo do.
    2. Ɔrenntsea mu, eso ɔremma ne ndze do, anaaso ɔremma wɔnntse ne ndze wɔ ɔbrɔn mu.
    3. Ndzɛmbir a akontom no, orummbu no, na asaaba a orupun wusiw no, orunndum no: obeyi atsɛmbu edzi wɔ nokwar mu.
    4. N'ano ronndwe eso ɔremmpa abaw, ekodu dɛ ɔdze atsɛmbu esi asaase do; na nsuano aman tweɔn ne mbra.
    5. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye yi, ɔno a ɔbobɔɔ ɔsorsor, na ɔtserɛtserɛɛw mu; ɔno a ɔyeyeer asaase na dza ofi mu ba; ɔno a ɔdze nkwahwea ma no do nkorɔfo, na ɔdze sunsum ma hɔn a wɔnenam mu:, #Ndwu 17.24
    6. Emi mara EWURADZE na mafrɛ wo wɔ ndzeyɛtsenenee mu, mesuo wo nsamu, na makora wo, na medze wo ayɛ ɔman ahyɛmu, ayɛ Amanamamfo kandzea;
    7. ama eebuebue enyiwa a efurafura, eyi ndaduafo efi efiadze, na hɔn a wɔtsetse sum mu efi mpokyerɛ dan mu.
    8. Emi mara nye EWURADZE; me dzin nye no: na meremmfa m'enyimnyam mma obi, na m'ayɛyi so meremmfa mma ehonyi a woesian.
    9. Hwɛ, adadadze no aba mu, na ndzɛmba afofor na meda no edzi: meka ho asɛm kyerɛ hom, ansaana woefifir.
    10. Hom ntow ndwom fofor mma EWURADZE, na hom mfi asaase ano noho ntow n'ayɛyindwom; hom a hom sian kɔfow po, na dza ɔwɔ mu nyina, nsuano aman, na no mu atsefo.
    11. Wɔmma sar na no do nkurow no mma hɔn ndze do, nkuroba a Kedar tse do no; wɔmma Selafo ntow enyigye ndwom, wɔmma womfi mbepɔw etsifi mbɔ ose.
    12. Wɔmma wɔnhyɛ EWURADZE enyimnyam, na wɔnda n'ayɛyi edzi wɔ nsuano aman mu.
    13. EWURADZE befir edzi dɛ ɔkatakyi; obekenyan nyinkun dɛ ɔsabarimba: ɔbɛtsea mu, nyew, ɔbɔbɔ ose; obedzi n'atamfo do akatakyisɛm.
    14. Maka m'ano ato mu akyɛr; mayɛ komm, na mesianka moho: afei dze mebɛtsea mu dɛ ɔbaa a ɔroko awoo; mebɛkyem na megu ahom prɛko.
    15. Mebɛma mbepɔw na akoko afomfɔn, na mama hɔn do nhabamba nyinara egunguan; na madan nsutsen no nsupruw, na mawewew nsutaae no.
    16. Na medze efurafo bɛfa ɔtsempɔn a wonnyim do no do aba; ɔkwan a wonnyim mu no mu na mibegya hɔn afa: mebɛma sum ayɛ kan wɔ hɔn enyim, na mbrɛ ɔyɛ nkyeakyeae no, matsentsen no. Ndzɛmba iyinom na mebɛyɛ, na meremmpa hɔn.
    17. Wɔbɛsan ekyir, hɔn enyi bɔto kɛsenara, hɔn a wɔtwer ehonyi a woesian hɔn a wɔse ehonyi a woegu dɛ, Hɛn abosom nye hom no.
    18. Etsitsifo, hom ntsie; na enyifurafo, hom nhwɛ, ma hom eehu.
    19. Woana yɛ onyifurafo, dɛ m'akowaa nko? Anaa otsitsifo, tse dɛ mo bɔfoe a mosoma no no? Woana na n'enyi efura tse dɛ nyia ɔnye me tse asomdwee mu no, anaa oefura tse dɛ EWURADZE n'akowaa no?
    20. Ɔwo ihu ndzɛmba pii, naaso ennhyɛ no nsew; n'aso ebue, naaso ɔnntse asɛm.
    21. Ɔsɔɔ EWURADZE enyi dɛ, ne ndzeyɛtsenenee ntsi, ohuhor ne mbra, na ɔma onya enyidzi.
    22. Na iyinom dze wɔyɛ aman a woetwa hɔn dwo na wɔafa hɔn afo; woesuasua hɔn nyinara mfir wɔ etu mu, na wɔdze hɔn esumasuma mpokyerɛfo adan mu: wɔayɛ afonam, na obi nngye hɔn nkwa; wɔayɛ asadze, na obi nnka dɛ, Fa san ma.
    23. Hom mu woana na ɔbɛma iyi aso? Ɔbɛkyɛn aso etsie ndaamba asɛm?
    24. Woana na ɔdze Jakob maa dɛ afonam, na ɔdze Israel maa edwotwafo no? Ana nnyɛ EWURADZE bi a? Ɔno a yɛayɛ bɔn etsia no, na n'akwan no, wɔammpɛ dɛ wɔnantsew mu, eso wɔannyɛ setsie amma ne mbra.
    25. Dɛm ntsi na ohuee n'ebufuhyew na ɔko ne dzendzen guu no do; na ɔtoo no gya hyiae, naaso oennhu; na ɔhyeew no, naaso ɔammfa annhyɛ no werɛ mu.

    Tsir 43

    1. Na afei mbrɛ EWURADZE a ɔbɔɔ wo, ao Jakob, na ɔno a ɔween wo, ao Israel, no se nye yi: Mma nnsuro, na mapon wo; mabɔ wo dzin afrɛ wo, eyɛ medze.
    2. Sɛ irutwa esu a, menye wo nam; sɛ idua esutsen mu a, orummunam wo: sɛ enam ogya mu a, ennkɛhyew; eso ogyaframee rennhyew wo.
    3. Na emi nye EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi, w'agyenkwa no; medze Egypt ayɛ w'apondze, medze Etiopia na Seba bɛsesa wo nkwa.
    4. Osiandɛ asom bo wɔ m'enyi do, na enya enyidzi, na modɔ wo ntsi, medze nyimpa bɛsesa wo tsir na medze aman besi wo nkwa ananmu.
    5. Mma nnsuro; na menye wo nam: medze w'asefo befi boka aba, na maboa wo ano efi anee;
    6. mebɛse kwaamu afamu dɛ, Fa ma; na pomu afamu dɛ, Mma nnkam do; fa me mba fi ekyirekyir, na me mbabaa fi asaase ano noho bra;
    7. nyew, obiara a wɔbɔ me dzin frɛ no, na mabɔ no ama m'enyimnyam no, nyia emi na moween no; na meyɛɛ no no.
    8. Hom mfa ɔman a wɔwɔ enyiwa naaso wɔyɛ efurafo, na etsitsifo a wɔwɔ aso no mbra.
    9. Amanaman nyinara mboaboa hɔn ano fakor, na nyimpa nyina nhyia mu: hɔn mu woana botum ada iyi edzi, na ɔakyerɛ nkankan no ndzɛmba? Wɔmma wɔmfa hɔn adasefo mbra, ma wondzi bem: anaa wɔmma wontsie, na wɔnka dɛ, Ɔyɛ nokwar.
    10. Homara nye m'adasefo, EWURADZE na ɔse, na m'akowaa a masan mu meyi no: ama hom eehu na wɔaagye me edzi, na wɔaatse ase dɛ emi nye ɔno; wɔnnhyehyɛɛ onyame bi nndzii m'enyim da, eso m'ekyir obi remmba pɛn.
    11. Emi, emi mara, nye EWURADZE; na Agyenkwa bi nnyi hɔ ka mo ho.
    12. Emi na medaa no edzi, gyee nkwa, na mekyerɛe, ber a nna anana nyame bi nnyi hom mu: na homara nye m'adasefo, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    13. Nyew, Emi nye Nyankopɔn, na ofitsi ndɛ kɔ so emi nye ɔno; obi nnyi hɔ a obotum agye efi me nsamu: midzi mo dwuma, na woana botum esiw mo kwan?
    14. Mbrɛ EWURADZE, hom Pomfo, Israel Krɔnkrɔn no, ɔse nye yi: Hom ntsi mobɔsoma akɔ Babilɔn, na mebubu adaban nyinara, na Kaldeafo no hɔn ehurusi bɛdan hɔn sukwadwom.
    15. Emi nye EWURADZE, hom Krɔnkrɔnnyi no, Israel no Bɔfo, na hom Hen no.
    16. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, ɔno a ɔma ɔtsempɔn da po mu, na ɔma ɔkwan da esu akɛse mu;
    17. ɔno a ɔdze ntseaseanam na pɔnkɔ, dɔm na tum fir edzi no; hɔn nyina bɔ mu deda famu, wonnkotum asoɛr; wɔasa, woedundum dɛ asaaba:
    18. mma hom nkaa nkan no ndzɛmba, eso mma hom ndwendwen tsetse ndzɛmba ho.
    19. Hwɛ, merebɛyɛ adze fofor; afei na orififir; aso hom nnhu? Mobɔbɔ ɔkwan ato sar do mpo, na esutsen wɔ sar pradada do.
    20. Hamu mbowa bedzi me nyi, mpataku na nsohor: osiandɛ mema nsu ba wɔ sar mu, na esutsen ba wɔ sar pradada mu, ama me man a masan mu meyi hɔn no wɔaanom.
    21. Ɔman no a mehyehyɛɛ hɔn maa mankasa moho no, ama woeeyi m'ayɛyi akyerɛ no a.
    22. Naaso ammfrɛ me, Ao Jakob; na mbom mo ho afon wo, Ao Israel.
    23. Emmfaa wo hyew afɔr nguan no mmbrɛɛ me; eso emmfaa w'afɔrbɔdze nndzii me nyi. Memmaa emmfaa w'edziban afɔr nnsoom me, eso memmaa emmberɛe wɔ nduhuam.
    24. Ɔwo emmfaa sika nntɔɔ ahwer mmaa me, eso emmaa w'afɔrbɔ seradze mmee me: mbom edze wo bɔn atseetsee me, edze w'emumuyɛ ama maberɛ.
    25. Emi, emi marankasa, nye nyia ɔpepa wo mbrato wɔ mankasa me ntsi; na merennkaa wo bɔn.
    26. Kaakaa me ɛ; ma yenyi atsɛn: ka w'asɛm, ama eedzi bem.
    27. W'egya a odzi kan no yɛɛ bɔn, na wo ntamugyinafo ato mbra etsia me.
    28. Dɛm ntsi megu krɔnkrɔnbea mbapɔmba no ho fi, na meyi Jakob ama ɔsɛɛ kɛse, na Israel ama asesardze.

    Tsir 44

    1. Naaso afei, m'akowaa Jakob, tsie; na Israel a masan mu meyi wo:
    2. Mbrɛ EWURADZE a ɔyɛɛ wo, na ɔhyehyɛɛ wo fii yafun mu na ɔbɔboa wo no, se nye yi: M'akowaa Jakob, mma nnsuro; na ɔwo, Jerusalɛm a masan mu meyi wo.
    3. Na mubohue nsu egu nyia nsukɔm dze no no do, na nsubansuba egu daadze kɛsɛɛ do: mubohue mo sunsum egu w'asefo do, na me nhyira egu hɔn a wofi wo mu do:
    4. na wobefifir nkyɛkyɛr ntamu, dɛ esuka do ndua.
    5. Obi bɛse dɛ, meyɛ EWURADZE dze; na obi so dze Jakob ne dzin afrɛ noho; na obi so bio dze ne nsa akyerɛw dɛ ɔyɛ EWURADZE dze, na ɔdze Israel ne dzin ato no do.
    6. Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Hen, na no pomfo, dɔm EWURADZE no, ɔse nye yi: Emi nye ɔkandzifo, na emi nye okyidzifo; na nyame bi nnyi hɔ ka mo ho.
    7. Woana na ɔtse dɛ emi? Ma ɔnka ɛ. Ma ɔmpaa mu nka mfa nsi m'enyim. Woana na ofi tsetseetse ɔakyerɛ ndzɛmba a ɔreba, na ɔman a medze besi hɔ no na dza ɔbɛba no? Wɔmma wɔnda dza ɔbɛba no edzi ɛ.
    8. Mma hom nnsuro, eso mma hom bo nntu: ana mimmfi tsetse na mekaa kyerɛɛ hom, na medze kyerɛe? Na homara nye m'adasefo. Aso Nyankopɔn bi wɔ hɔ ka mo ho? Ɛhɛɛ, Ɔbotan bi nnyi hɔ; minnyim biara.
    9. Hɔn a wɔyɛ ohonyi a woesian nyinara yɛ egyangyandze; na hɔn enyigyedze ho nnkɛba mfaso: na hɔnankasa hɔn adasefo runnhu adze, eso wonnyim adze; ama hɔn enyi aato.
    10. Woana na ɔayɛ bosom, anaa oegu ohonyi a woesian a mfaso bi nnyi ho?
    11. Hwɛ, nsɛfo nyinara enyi bɔtoto; na edwimfo no, adasamba yi ara bi a: wɔmma hɔn nyinara wɔmboa ano fakor, wɔmma wongyinagyina hɔ; wobosuro, hɔn enyi bɔto prɛko.
    12. Ɔtomfo bɔ ekuma, na ɔyɛ ngyabiriw mu edwuma, na ɔdze nhamɛr bor no, na ɔdze n'abaw dzendzen yɛ ho edwuma: nyew, ɔkɔm dze no, na n'ahoɔdzen pa; ɔnnom nsu, na ɔtɔ bitsi.
    13. Duadwimfo dze ahoma to; ɔdze ntwoma sensan; ɔdze twerɛw ndadze siesie ho, na ɔdze kɔmpase sensan ho, na osian no nyimpa saso, dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa n'ahoɔfɛw tse, ma ɔaatsena dan no mu.
    14. Ɔtow nkyindur ndua, na ɔfa abrɔwi na osudur, na ɔhyɛ kwaa mu ndua bi dzen ma noho: ɔtsɛw nkyindur ndua, na nyankonsu nyɛn no.
    15. Nna nkyii ɔbɛyɛ dza nyimpa dze kua ogya; na ɔfa bi na ɔdze to hyew; nyew, okua, na ɔto boodoo: nyew, ɔyɛ bosom, na ɔsom no; ɔyɛ no ohonyi a woesian, na ɔkotow no.
    16. Ɔsɔ ne fa bi ogya mu; ɔdze ne fa bi so dzi nam; ɔkyew nam, na odzidzi mee: nyew, ɔto so, ma ɔka dɛ, Yɛɛ, mo ho ayɛ me hyew ae, ogya na mehu yi.
    17. Ne nkaa no ɔdze yɛ bosom bi, no honyi a woesian no a: ɔkotow no, na ɔsɔr no, na oyi no mpaa, na ɔka dɛ, Gye me; na ɔwo nye me nyame.
    18. Wonnyim, eso wɔnndwen ho: osiandɛ ɔaseram hɔn enyi, ma wonntum nnhu; na hɔn akoma, ma wonntum nntse ase.
    19. Na obiara nnkaa, eso nyimdzee anaa ntseasee bi nnyi hɔ a ɔdze bɛse dɛ, Masɔ ne fa bi wɔ ogya mu; nyew, medze ne gyabiriw bi ato boodoo; makyew nam na medzi: na aso medze ne nkaa no mebɛyɛ ewurkadze? Aso mobɔkotow duasin?
    20. Nso na odzi: akoma a wɔadaadaa no no dze no aman nkyɛn, na onntum nngye ne kra, anaa ɔnnka dɛ, Aso nnyɛ ator na ɔwɔ me nsa nyimfa mu yi?
    21. Ao Jakob, kaa ndzɛmba yinom; na Israel, osiandɛ ɔwo nye m'akowaa: emi na mahyehyɛ wo; ɔwo nye n'akowaa. Ao Israel, mo werɛ nnkefir wo.
    22. Mapepa wo mbrato, dɛ mununkum kumbɔɔ, na wo ndzebɔn, dɛ nsuwusiw: san bra me nkyɛn; na mapon wo.
    23. Ɔsorsor, hom ntow ndwom, na EWURADZE na ɔayɛ; asaase ase noho, hom mbɔ ose; mbepɔw, kwaa, na ndua a ɔwɔ mu nyinara, hom mfa ehurusi ndwom: na EWURADZE apon Jakob, na ɔbɛhyɛ noho enyimnyam wɔ Israel mu.
    24. Mbrɛ EWURADZE, wo pomfo, na nyia ɔhyehyɛɛ wo fii yafun mu no, ɔse nye yi: Emi nye EWURADZE a ɔyɛ ndzɛmba nyinara no; no nko ara twe ɔsorsor mu; na ɔtserɛw asaase mu; woana ka mo ho?
    25. Nyia ɔma atorfo nsɛnkyerɛdze yɛ gyan, na ɔma ebisatsirfo bobɔ adam; nyia ɔma enyansafo san ekyirekyir, na ɔyɛ hɔn nyimdzee nkwaseasɛm:
    26. nyia ɔhyɛ n'akowaa n'asɛm dzen, na ɔma n'abɔfoe hɔn apam ba mu; nyia ɔka wɔ Jerusalɛm ho dɛ, Wɔbɛtsena no mu; na wɔ Juda nkurow no ho dɛ, Wɔbɛkyekyer, na mamema n'ekurofo no do:
    27. nyia ɔse bun no dɛ, Wew, na mebɛma w'esutsen awewew:
    28. nyia ɔka wɔ Sirus ho dɛ, Mo guanhwɛfo nye no, na ɔbɛma mo botae nyina ayɛ hɔ: ɔbɛka wɔ Jerusalɛm ho mpo dɛ, Wɔbɛkyekyer; na asɔrfi no ho dɛ, Wɔbotow wo fapem.

    Tsir 45

    1. Dɛm na EWURADZE ka kyerɛ ne nyia ɔasera no, Sirus a mesuo ne nsa nyimfa mu dɛ mebɛbrɛ amanaman adze wɔ n'enyim, na masansan ahemfo asen; dɛ mubobuebue mbobow wɔ n'enyim, na aponkɛse no wɔanntotow mu.
    2. Emi mara mibedzi w'enyim akɔ, na mama mbea a ayɛ kekakeka no ayɛ dɛfɛɛ: mubobubu boran mbobow no mu esinesin, na metwitwa adaban no mu.
    3. Medze sum mu akoradze, na ehuntsambea ahonyadze a wɔdze esuma bɛma wo, ama eehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no a mobɔ wo dzin frɛ wo no.
    4. Osian m'akowaa Jakob, na Israel a masan mu eyi no ntsi, mobɔ wo dzin frɛ wo: mato wo ebusuadzin, kaansa ɔwo nnhun me mpo a.
    5. Emi nye EWURADZE, na obi nnyi hɔ bio; Nyankopɔn bi nnyi hɔ ka mo ho: mobɔbɔ wo abɔdo, kaansa ɔwo nnhun me mpo a:
    6. ama wofi wipuei ɔnye anee eehu, dɛ obi nnyi hɔ ka mo ho: emi nye EWURADZE, na obi nnyi hɔ bio.
    7. Emi na mehyehyɛ kan, na mobɔ sum; emi na meyɛ asomdwee, na mobɔ mbusu; emi nye EWURADZE a ɔyɛ ndzɛmba yinom nyinara.
    8. Ɔsorsor, hom mfi ɔsor nsosɔw, na hom mma wimu ntɔ ndzeyɛtsenenee ngu: asaase mbuebue, ma wɔmma nkwagye mbra, na ɔmma ɔnye ndzeyɛtsenenee mbɔ mu mfifir; emi EWURADZE na mabɔ.
    9. Nyia ɔnye no Bɔfo dzi esi no, ondue! Asaase do ntankofɛr mu ɔtankofɛr! Aso awendɛtse bɛse nyia ɔwen no no dɛ, Ereyɛ dɛn nye yi? Anaa w'edwuma no nnyi nsa?
    10. Nyia ɔse n'egya dɛ, Ebɛnadze na awo no yi, anaa ɔbaa dɛ, Ebɛnadze na ekoo no awoo yi no ondue!
    11. Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi, na no Bɔfo no se nye yi: Hom mbisa me ndzɛmba a ɔbɛba ho asɛm; hom nhyɛ me mbra wɔ me mbabanyin ho, na me nsaano edwuma ho.
    12. Emi na mayɛ asaase, na mabɔ nyimpa wɔ do: emi, me nsa ara a, na matwetwe ɔsorsor mu, na hɔn dɔm nyinara emi na mahyɛ.
    13. Emi na mama no do wɔ ndzeyɛtsenenee mu, na mebɛtsentsen n'akwan nyinara: ɔno na ɔbɛkyekyer mo kurow, na ɔama m'amantufo afa hɔn ho tɔtrɔtɔ, nnyɛ tsibo bi anaa akatua bi ntsi, dɔm EWURADZE na ɔse.
    14. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Egypt edwumadze, na Etiopia eguadze, na Sabeafo, mbarimba akraban, wobotwa mu aba wo nkyɛn, na wɔbɛyɛ wodze; wobedzi w'ekyir; mpokyerɛ mu na wobotwa mu aba: na wɔbɔkotow wo, wobedzi wo nkotoserɛ, dɛ Ampaara, Nyankopɔn wɔ wo mu; na obi nnyi hɔ bio, Nyankopɔn bi nnyi hɔ.
    15. Nokwar ara, ɔwo nye Nyankopɔn a ihuntsa woho, Israel Nyankopɔn, Agyenkwa no.
    16. Hɔn nyinara, hɔn enyi bɔto, nyew, hɔn enyim bogu ase: hɔn a wɔyɛ ehonyi nyina bɔbɔ mu ahyɛ ahoraa.
    17. Na Israel dze, EWURADZE dze ɔdomankoma nkwagye agye no nkwa: hom enyi ronnto, eso hom enyim runngu ase ara daapem.
    18. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE a ɔbɔɔ ɔsorsor no se nye yi; ɔno nye Nyankopɔn; nyia ɔhyehyɛɛ asaase na ɔyɛe; ɔno na ɔdze tsiim hɔ, ɔammbɔ no pan, ɔhyehyɛe ama wɔaatsena mu: emi nye EWURADZE; na obi nnyi hɔ bio.
    19. Nnyɛ nsumaa mu, sum mu asaase beebi, na makasa; mannse Jakob asefo dɛ, Hom nhwehwɛ me basabasayɛ mu: emi EWURADZE, mekasa ndzeyɛtsenenee, meka ndzɛmba a ɔtsen kyerɛ.
    20. Hom nhyiahyia hom ho na hom mbra; hom mbɔ mu ntwe mbɛn, hom a hom efi nsa wɔ amanaman mu: hɔn a wɔsoso hɔn ehonyi a woesian no ndua, na woyi mpaa ma onyame a onntum nngye nkwa no, wonnyim dze.
    21. Hom nka nkyerɛ, na wɔmma ompue, nyew, wɔmma wɔmbɔ mu ntu egyina; woana na ofi tsetseberdo ɔakyerɛ iyi? Woana na ɔaka yi akyerɛ dadaada? Aso nnyɛ emi EWURADZE a? Na nyame bi nnyi hɔ ka mo ho; pɛrpɛr Nyankopɔn na Agyenkwa; obi nnyi hɔ ka mo ho.
    22. Asaase ewiei nyinara, hom ndan mbra mo hɔ, na hom nnya nkwa: osiandɛ emi nye Nyankopɔn, na obi nnyi hɔ bio.
    23. Maka mara moho ntam, asɛm no efi m'anomu kɔ wɔ ndzeyɛtsenenee mu, na ɔnnkɛsan, dɛ emi na anankoroma nyinara bɔkotow me, na tɛkyerɛma nyinara bɛka me ntam., #Rom 14.11; Fil 2.10
    24. Obi bɛse dɛ, EWURADZE mu ara nko na ndzeyɛtsenenee na ahoɔdzen wɔ: ne nkyɛn ara na adasa bɛba, na hɔn a hɔn bo fuuw no nyinara hɔn enyi bɔto.
    25. EWURADZE mu na Israel asefo nyinara bedzi bem, na wɔahyehyɛ hɔnho.

    Tsir 46

    1. Bel butuw, Nebo kotow; hɔn ehonyi soso adzesoa mbowa, na anantwi: ndzɛmba a hom soso no yɛ dur, adzesoa durdur ma mbowa a wɔaberɛ.
    2. Wɔkotow, wɔbɔ mu butuw; wonnkotum eyi adzesoa durdur no, na hɔnankasa wɔkɔ ndɔmmum mu.
    3. Jakob fifo, hom nyɛ aso mma me, na Israel fie nkaa nyinara hɔn a metur hɔn fi yafun mu, masoa hɔn fi awotoa mu:
    4. na ɔdze kodu nkɔdaayɛ mu mpo emi nye no, na ɔdze kodu gon no mfuwii mu mpo, mobɔbɔ wo akɔnkɔn: emi na mayɛ wo, na mubotur wo; nyew, mobɔbɔ wo akɔnkɔn, na magye wo.
    5. Woana na hom dze me bɔto no ho, ma menye no ayɛ pɛr, na hom dze me bosusu, ma yaasɛ?
    6. Hɔn a wohue sika fi foto mu, na woker dwetɛ wɔ nsɛn mu, wɔma sikadwinnyi apɛnsa, na ɔdze yɛ ɔbosom; wɔkotow, nyew, wɔsɔr no.
    7. Wɔbɔ no akɔnkɔn, wɔsoa no, na wɔdze no kesi ne sibea, na ogyina hɔ; onnkotum efi ne sibea efi: nyew, sɛ obi tsea mu frɛ no a, onntum mmbua, anaaso ɔnngye no mmfi no fona mu.
    8. Hom nkaa iyi, na hom ndwendwen ho, hom mbarimba mbratofo, hom nkaakaa.
    9. Hom nkaakaa kankan tsetse ndzɛmba no: osiandɛ emi nye Nyankopɔn, na obi nnyi hɔ bio; emi nye Nyankopɔn, na obi nnyi hɔ tse dɛ emi a, ISA.46.10, mifi ahyɛse meka ewiei no mekyerɛ, na mifi tsetseber do meka dza wonnyae nnyɛe no kyerɛ; dɛ, M'apam begyina, na mebɛyɛ m'ahyehyɛ nyinara.
    10. Mebɛfrɛ anoma edzinam bi efi boka, m'apam mu banyin efi ekyirekyir asaase do; ɛhɛɛ, makasa, mebɛma aba mu so; mabɔ tsirmpɔw, mebɛyɛ so.
    11. Akokobirfo hom ntsie me, hom a hom ntamu nye ɔgye twe:
    12. medze me tsenenee abɛn, ɔronnkɔ ekyirekyir bio, na mo nkwagye rinnkyinkyim; na medze nkwagye bɔto Zion ama m'enyimnyam Israel.

    Tsir 47

    1. Babilɔn babaa ɔbaabun e, sian na tsena huntuma mu; Ao Kaldeafo babaa e, kwetsir ahengua tsena daadze: na wɔnnkɛda ho afrɛ wo bɔkɔbɔkɔnyi na ɔhosɔrnyi bio.
    2. Fa ewuyambo no, na yam ewu: yi wo nkataenyim, pɔr w'asensɛnekyir no gu, pata w'anantu ho, twa nsutsen.
    3. W'adagyaw bɛda edzi, nyew, wobohu w'ahoto. Mibedzi wer, na merenngye nyimpa biara.
    4. Hɛn pomfo no, ne dzin dze dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no.
    5. Kaldeafo babaa, tsena hɔ komm, na kɔ sum no mu: na wɔnnkɛda ho afrɛ wo ahendzi horow ewuraba bio.
    6. Mo bo fuuw me man, muguu m'egyapadze ho fi, na medze hɔn hyɛɛ wo nsa: ɔwo ennhu hɔn mbɔbɔr biara; edze wo kɔndua ato nkɔdaa do duduudur.
    7. Na ekaa dɛ, Mebɛyɛ ewuraba daa: ma dɛm ntsi ammfa ndzɛmba yinom annto w'akoma mu, eso annkaa n'ewiei.
    8. Dɛm ntsi afei tsie iyi, ɔwo a edze woho ama enyigyedze, emmfa dze nnyɛ dze, eka no w'akoma mu dɛ, Emi mara a, na obi nnyi hɔ ka mo ho; merenntsena dɛ okunafo, eso mirinndzi awo mba wu:, #Nyi 18.7
    9. naaso ndzɛmba ebien yi bɛba wo do awora da kor, awo mba wu na ekunayɛ: wɔbɛba wo do ma ara tɔ, wɔ w'abayisɛm dodow, na w'adzeafosɛm a ɔdɔɔ so pii no nyina ekyir.
    10. Na ɔwo edze wo werɛ atwer w'emumuyɛ; aka dɛ, Obi nnhu me; wo nyansaa na wo nyimdzee akyea w'adwen: na aka wɔ w'akoma mu dɛ, Emi mara a, na obi nnyi hɔ ka mo ho.
    11. Dɛm ntsi mbusu bɔto wo; innkohu ne mbae; na atoyerɛnkyɛm bɔto wo; irunntum nnyi nngu: na ɔsɛɛ bɛba wo do awora a innyim.
    12. Afei fa w'adzeafosɛm soɛr gyina ɛ, ɔnye w'abayifosɛm dodow a ifi wo mbofrabermu aberɛ mu no; egyangyanbiara ibotum dze enya mfaso bi, egyangyanbiara edze bedzi nyim bi.
    13. Aberɛ wɔ w'egyinatu dodow mu: afei ma ɔsor enyi nkyekyɛmufo, nworabahwɛfo, abosoom horow ho adzekyerɛfo no nsoɛr na wɔngye wo nkwa mfi ndzɛmba a ɔbɛba wo do no mu.
    14. Hwɛ, wɔbɛyɛ dɛ eburonan; ogya no bɛhyew hɔn; wonnkotum agye hɔnho efi ogyaframee no n'ahoɔdzen nsa: ɔrennyɛ ogyabiriw a wɔto bi, anaa ogya a wɔko ho.
    15. Dɛm na ndzɛmba a aberɛ wɔ mu no bɛyɛ ama wo: hɔn a ofitsi wo mbofrabermu wɔnye wo edzi gua no bekyin akokɔ hɔn abrɔn mu; obiara nnyi hɔ a ɔbɛgye wo nkwa.

    Tsir 48

    1. Hom ntsie iyi, ao Jakob fifo hom a wɔato hom dzin Israel, na hom fi Juda esu mu epue; hom a hom dze EWURADZE dzin ka ntam, na hom bɔ Israel Nyankopɔn ne dzin, naaso nnyɛ nokwar, anaa tsenenee mu.
    2. Na wɔfrɛ hɔnho dɛ wofi kurow krɔnkrɔn no mu, na wɔdze hɔnho twer Israel Nyankopɔn; ne dzin dze dɔm EWURADZE.
    3. Mifi tsetse na maka kan ndzɛmba no akyerɛ; ampaara, wofi m'anomu firii, na medze kyerɛe: awerɛfir mu ara na meyɛe, na wɔbaa mu.
    4. Osiandɛ minyim dɛ eyɛ ntsintsiman, na wo kɔn yɛ dadze ntsin, na wo momapɔw yɛ boran;
    5. ntsi na mifi tsetse maka akyerɛ wo; medze kyerɛɛ wo ansaana ɔaba mu: amma ɔwoara aannka dɛ, Mo honyi na ɔayɛ, na mo honyi a woesian, na m'ehonyi a woegu na wɔhyɛe.
    6. Ɔwoara atse; afei hwɛ iyi nyina; na hom, ana hom nnkɛka akyerɛ? Makyerɛ wo ndzɛmba afofor ofitsi ndɛ, mekyerɛ esumadze a innhunii.
    7. Afei na wɔabɔ hɔn, na ommfi tsetse; na ɔdze bodu ndɛ, enntsee da; amma aannka dɛ, Hwɛ, minyim.
    8. Nntsee da; nyew, innhunii; nyew, ofir tsetse na w'asowa emmbue: osiandɛ muhun dɛ ɔwo ibotwa nkontompɔ papaara, na wɔfrɛɛ wo mbratonyi fir yafun mu.
    9. Me dzin ntsi na mibekyinkyim m'ebufuw, na m'ayɛyi ntsi na mobɔbɔ wo ho esianka, amma meennkruw w'ase.
    10. Hwɛ, manan wo, na nnyɛ dɛ dwetɛ; medze wo afa ahohiahia fononoo mu epue.
    11. Mara me ntsi a, mara me ntsi a, na meyɛ; na ɔbɛyɛ dɛn bɛyɛ dɛ wobogu me dzin ho fi? Na meremmfa m'enyimnyam mma obi.
    12. Jakob, tsie me ɛ, na Israel a mafrɛ wo: emi nye ɔno; emi nye ɔkandzifo, emi ara so nye okyidzifo.
    13. Me nsa na ɔtoow asaase ne fapem, na me nsa enyimfa na ɔtserɛɛw ɔsorsor mu: sɛ mefrɛ hɔn a, wɔsoɛr gyina prɛko.
    14. Hom nyinara, hom mboa hom ano, na hom ntsie; hom mu woana na ɔaka ndzɛmba yinom akyerɛ? EWURADZE dɔ no: ɔbɛyɛ dza ɔahyehyɛ wɔ Babilɔn do, na n'abaw bɛda Kaldeafo do.
    15. Emi, emi mara, na makasa; nyew, emi na mafrɛ no: medze no aba, na no kwan bɛyɛ prɔmprɔm.
    16. Hom ntwe mbɛn me, hom ntsie iyi; ofitsi ahyɛse ara mennkasaa nsumaa mu; ofitsi ber a ɔbae ara, na mowɔ hɔ: na afei EWURADZE Nyankopɔn asoma emi, na no Sunsum.
    17. Mbrɛ EWURADZE, wo pomfo, Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no, ɔse nye yi: Emi nye EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn a ɔkyerɛkyerɛ wo ma wo mfaso, na ogya wo wɔ ɔkwan a ewɔ dɛ efa do no mu.
    18. Ao kɛtseankyɛ eyɛɛ aso maa me mbransɛm! Nkyɛ w'asomdwee ayɛ dɛ esutsen, na wo tsenenee ayɛ dɛ po asorɛkye.
    19. Nkyɛ w'asefo so ayɛ dɛ anhwea, na wo nson mu aba so ayɛ dɛ anhweaabo: worunntwa ne dzin nnkyen; eso wɔrennsɛɛ no mmfi m'enyim.
    20. Hom mfi Babilɔn mfi, hom nguan mfi Kaldeafo mu; hom mfa adwontow ndze nka nkyerɛ, hom nka iyi, hom mbɔ dzin nkodu asaase ewiei mpo: hom nse dɛ, EWURADZE apon n'akowaa Jakob.
    21. Na nsukɔm anndze hɔn ber a ogyaa hɔn duaa sar pradada do no: ɔmaa esu fii ɔbotan mu pemee maa hɔn: ɔpaa ɔbotan mu so, na esu no gyee punkum.
    22. Asomdwee bi nnyi hɔ mma emumuyɛfo, EWURADZE na ɔse.

    Tsir 49

    1. Nsuano aman, hom ntsie me; na aman a wofi ekyirekyir, hom nyɛ aso: EWURADZE afrɛ me fitsi awotoa mu; ofi me na no nson mu na ɔabɔ me dzin:
    2. na ɔayɛ m'ano dɛ afona ndam ndam, ne nsaano nwinwin mu na ɔdze me ehuntsa; na ɔdze me ayɛ egyen a wɔapɔw ho, n'egyen kotoku mu na ɔdze me esie:
    3. na ɔsee me dɛ, M'akowaa nye wo; Israel a mebɛhyɛ moho enyimnyam wɔ wo mu.
    4. Na mekaa dɛ, Maberɛ kwa, mahwer m'ahoɔdzen ama adzehun na egyangyandze: naaso m'atsɛmbu wɔ EWURADZE nsamu, na me nhyɛananmu wɔ me Nyankopɔn nsamu.
    5. Na afei EWURADZE a ɔhyehyɛɛ me fii awotoa mu dɛ mebɛyɛ n'akowaa, na memfa Jakob nsan mbra no, na dɛ wɔmboaboa Israel ano mbrɛ no no, osiandɛ menya enyidzi wɔ EWURADZE enyi do, na me Nyankopɔn abɛyɛ m'ahoɔdzen:
    6. Nyew, ɔdɛ, Ɔyɛ tootooba dɛ ebɛyɛ m'akowaa a ɔbɛma Jakob mbusuakuw do, na ɔdze Israel mu hɔn a wɔakora hɔn do no asan aba: eso medze wo bɛma Amanamamfo dɛ hɔn kandzea, ama aayɛ mo nkwa ekesi asaase ewiei.
    7. Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel pomfo, na no Krɔnkrɔnnyi no, ɔka kyerɛ nyia ɔdasanyi bu no enyimtsia, na ɔman no kyir no, ahyɛdofo akowaa no nye yi: Ahemfo bohu na wɔasoɛrsoɛr; mbapɔmba, na wɔasɔr; osian EWURADZE a odzi asɛnkor, mekyerɛ Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi a ɔasan mu eyi wo ntsi.
    8. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Aber a ɔsɛ mu na magye wo do, na nkwagye da mu na maboa wo: na mobɔkora wo do, na medze wo ama dɛ ɔman ahyɛmudzi, ma aama asaase no do esi hɔ, ma aama woenya egyapadze a wɔayeyɛ afo no edzi;
    9. ma aaka akyerɛ hɔn a wogugu nkyehoma mu no dɛ, Hom mfir nkɔ; na hɔn a wɔwɔ sum mu no, dɛ, Hom nyi homho nkyerɛ. Wobedzidzi akwan do, na mpampaa pataa nyinara do bɛyɛ hɔn edzidzibea.
    10. Ɔkɔm anaa nsukɔm renndze hɔn; eso ɔhyew anaa ewia rennka hɔn: na nyia ohu hɔn mbɔbɔr no obegya hɔn kwan, mbrɛ mbasu wɔ mpo na obegya hɔn afa.
    11. Na mebɛyɛ me mbepɔw nyinara ɔkwan, na m'atsempɔn akrɔnkrɔn.
    12. Hwɛ, woyinom wofi ekyirekyir bɛba: na, hwɛ, woyinom wofi kwaamu afamu na anee; na woyinom wofi Sinim asaase do.
    13. Ɔsorsor, hom ntow ndwom; asaase, dzi ehurusi; na mbepɔw, hom mfa ehurusi ndwom: na EWURADZE akyekye ne man hɔn werɛ, ne yamu bɛhyehye no wɔ n'amandzehufo ho.
    14. Naaso Zion see dɛ, EWURADZE apow me, na m'EWURADZE no werɛ efir me.
    15. Aso ɔbaa no werɛ befir no numfoanoba araa ma ne yamu nnkɛhyehye no wɔ ba a ofi n'awotoa mu no ho? Nyew, annyɛ a woyinom hɔn werɛ befir, naaso emi dze, mo werɛ nnkefir wo da.
    16. Hwɛ, mekrukye wo wɔ me nsayamu; w'afasu wɔ m'enyim daa.
    17. Wo nkurokyekyerfo hɔn ho yɛ har sen w'asɛɛfo na hɔn a wɔyɛɛ wo afo no wobefi wo nkyɛn akɔ.
    18. Ma w'enyi do bɔ aprɔw, na hwɛ: woyinom nyinara wɔboa hɔn ano kor, na wɔba wo nkyɛn. Dɛ metse ase yi, EWURADZE na ɔse, ɔhyehyɛ ara na edze hɔn bɛhyehyɛ woho dɛ ahyehyɛdze, na edze hɔn abɔ woho do, dɛ ayefor.
    19. Na, w'amamfo na wo nkurow a abobɔ na w'asaase a wɔasɛɛ no dze, ampaara afei ebɛyɛ kyekyerbaa ama no do atsefo, na hɔn a wɔmemen wo no bɔkɔ ekyirekyir.
    20. Mba a wɔwoo hɔn w'awerɛhow mu no benya aka wɔ w'asomu dɛ, Bea no suar ma me: ma me beebi ma mentsena.
    21. Ɔno na ebɛka no w'akoma mu dɛ, Woana na ɔawo woyinom ama me, ber a wɔagye me mba efi me nsa, na mayɛ ankonam, ɔmantunyi a morowona kɔ ba? Na woana na ɔatsetse woyinom? Hwɛ, ɔkaa mankotsee; woyinom, henfa na nkyɛ wɔwɔ?
    22. Mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye yi, Hwɛ, mebɛma me nsa do makyerɛ amanaman, na mesi me frankaa akyerɛ aman: na wobotur wo mbabanyin wɔ hɔn bo mu aba, na wɔabɔ wo mbabaa akɔnkɔn.
    23. Na ahemfo bɛyɛ egyanom a wɔgyegye mba ama wo, na hɔn ahembaa ayɛ nanom a wɔgyegye mba ama wo: wɔbɔbɔ hɔn mu adze ama wo wɔdze hɔn enyim ebutubutuw famu, na wɔatafer w'anan ho huntuma; na ibohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE, na hɔn a wɔtweɔn me no hɔn enyim runngu ase.
    24. Aso wɔbɛgye ɔkatakyi ne nsamu afonam, anaa wɔdze ndɔmmum kwan mu bɛma?
    25. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Ɔkatakyi no ndɔmmum mpo wɔbɛgye akɔ, na etsiɔdzemfo afonam befi nsa: na emi dze menye hɔn a wɔnye wo si besi, na magye wo mba nkwa.
    26. Na mebɛma hɔn a wɔtseetsee wo no edzi hɔnankasa hɔn honam; na wɔanom hɔnankasa hɔn bɔgyaa abow, dɛ nsa fenemfenem; na adasa nyinara bohu dɛ emi EWURADZE nye w'agyenkwa na wo pomfo, Jakob ne Katakyi no.

    Tsir 50

    1. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Awargyaa nwoma a medze gyaa hom na awar no wɔ henfa? Anaa m'adzefirfo mu woana na matɔn hom ama no? Hwɛ, hom emumuyɛ ntsi na wɔtɔɔn hom, na hom mbrato ntsi na wogyaa hom na awar.
    2. Ebɛn ntsi na mebae a, obi nnyi hɔ? Mefrɛe a, obi nnyi hɔ a ɔgye do? Aso me nsa yɛ tsia, ma onnkotum apon? Anaa minnyi tum a wɔdze gye nkwa? Hwɛ, meka enyim a, mema po wew, mema nsutsen dandan sar: hɔn mu nam bombɔn, osiandɛ nsu nnyi hɔ ntsi, na wowuwu wɔ nsukɔm ntsi.
    3. Medze tuntum mefura ɔsorsor, na medze eyitam ayɛ hɔn nkataenyi.
    4. EWURADZE Nyankopɔn ama me hɔn a wɔakyerɛkyerɛ hɔn no hɔn tɛkyerɛma, ma meehu mbrɛ medze nsɛm bɔwowaw nyia ɔaberɛ: onyan anapa anapa, onyan m'aso ma maatse asɛm dɛ hɔn a wɔakyerɛkyerɛ hɔn.
    5. EWURADZE Nyankopɔn ebue m'aso, na manntsew etua, eso mannsan m'ekyir.
    6. Medze m'ekyir maa abobɔfo, na medze m'afon memaa hɔn a wotutu nhwi: mennhuntsa m'enyim emmfi fɛr na ntafi ho.
    7. Na EWURADZE Nyankopɔn bɔboa me; dɛm ntsi na m'enyim nngu ase yi: dɛm ntsi na mepirim m'enyim dɛ ɔtwerɛbo yi, na minyim dɛ m'enyim runngu ase.
    8. Nyia obu me bem no, ɔbɛn; woana na ɔnye me bedzi esi? Wɔmma yɛmbɔ mu ngyina: woana na ɔyɛ me tamfo? Ma ɔntwe mpin me.
    9. Hwɛ, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn bɔboa me; woana nye nyia obobu me fɔ? Hwɛ, hɔn nyinara bosuw dɛ atar; nkakraka bɔwe hɔn.
    10. Woana wɔ hom mu a osuro EWURADZE, na otsie n'akowaa ne ndze? Nyia ɔnantsew sum mu, na onnyi kan no, ma ɔmfa no werɛ nhyɛ EWURADZE ne dzin mu, na ɔndan ne Nyankopɔn.
    11. Hwɛ, hom a hom kuakua gya, hom dze ngyantsia yeyɛ abɔdo nyinara: hom nnantsew hom gya ne framee, ɔnye ngyantsia a hom asosɔ no mu. Iyi na hom benya no wɔ me nsamu; hom bɛdeda hɔ awerɛhow mu.

    Tsir 51

    1. Hom a hom dzi ndzeyɛtsenenee ekyir, hom a hom hwehwɛ EWURADZE, hom nyɛ aso mma me: hom nhwɛ ɔbotan a wɔpaa hom fii mu, na maa a wotuu hom fii mu no no tokur no.
    2. Hom nhwɛ hom egya Abraham, na Sara a ɔwoo hom no: ber a ɔyɛ ɔbaakofo no na mefrɛɛ no, na mihyiraa no, na meyɛɛ no ɔdodow.
    3. Na EWURADZE akyekye Zion no werɛ, na ɔama ne sar do ayɛ dɛ Eden, ne sar pradada ayɛ dɛ EWURADZE no ture; wobohu enyigye na ahosɛpɛw wɔ mu, ndaase, na adwontow ndze bɛba hɔ.
    4. Mo nkorɔfo, hom ntsie me; me man, hom nyɛ aso mma me: na mbra bi befi me nkyɛn akɔ, na mama m'atsɛmbu etsim hɔ ayɛ kan ama aman.
    5. Me tsenenee abɛn, mo nkwagye efir edzi, na m'abasa bobu aman atsɛn; nsuano aman bɔtweɔn me, na m'abasa do na wɔbɔtwer.
    6. Hom mma hom enyi do nhwɛ ɔsorsor, na hom nhwɛ asaase do wɔ famu: na ɔsorsor bɛhera dɛ wusiw, na asaase bosuw dɛ atar, na hɔn a wɔtsetse do no ewuwu dɛmara: na mo nkwagye dze, ɔbɛtsena hɔ daa, na me tsenenee wɔrennsɛɛ no.
    7. Hom a hom nyim tsenenee, ɔman a me mbra wɔ hom akoma mu, hom nyɛ aso mma me; mma hom nnsuro adasa hɔn ahorohoraa, eso mma hɔn ntom mma hom akoma nntu.
    8. Na nkakraka bɔwe hɔn dɛ atar, na abowaba awe hɔn dɛ kuntu: na me tsenenee dze, ɔbɛtsena hɔ daa na mo nkwagye edu mbasantsen nyinara do.
    9. EWURADZE ne basa e, nyan ɛ, nyan ɛ, fa ahoɔdzen hyɛ! Nyan, dɛ mpanyin ber no mu, tsetseberdo mbusuasantsen no mu. Ana nnyɛ ɔwo na itwitwaa Rahab mu esinesin, ihwiraa esuboa kɛse no mu no?
    10. Ana nnyɛ ɔwo na eweew po, bun kɛse n'esu no; edze po n'ebun no yɛɛ kwan maa hɔn a wɔapon hɔn no dɛ wontwa no?
    11. Hɔn a EWURADZE atɔ hɔn tsir no, wɔbɛsan, na wɔdze adwontow aba Zion; na ɔdomankoma dɛw bɛtsena hɔn etsifi: wobenya ahosɛpɛw na enyigye, na awerɛhow na nkrumsi eguan akɔ.
    12. Emi, mara, nye nyia ɔkyekye hom werɛ: ɔwo nye woana, na isuro ɔdasanyi a obowu, na ɔdasanyi ne ba a wɔbɛma ɔayɛ dɛ nkyɛkyɛr;
    13. na wo werɛ efir EWURADZE wo Bɔfo ɔno a ɔtserɛɛw ɔsorsor mu, na ɔdze asaase ne mfapem totoe; na eda ho suro daa wɔ ɔhyɛdofo no n'ebufuhyew ntsi, ber a osiesie noho dɛ ɔbɛsɛɛ? Na ɔhyɛdofo no n'ebufuhyew wɔ hen?
    14. Wɔbɛsan mpokyerɛnyi no ntsɛntsɛm; na onnkowu na oesian akɔ mona no mu, eso n'edziban nnkɔbɔ no.
    15. Na emi nye EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn a onunu po mu, ma n'asorɛkye wor: dɔm EWURADZE nye ne dzin.
    16. Na medze me nsɛm ahyɛ w'ano, na medze me nsa ho no nwinwin akata wo do, ama maatsetsɛw ɔsorsor, na maatoto asaase ne mfapem, na maase Zion dɛ, Ɔwo nye me man.
    17. Nyan ɛ, nyan ɛ, soɛr gyina ɛ, Jerusalɛm a anom EWURADZE nsamu n'ebufuhyew kɔɔpow no; ɔwo na anom ntentanto kɔɔpow no, na ehwiew mu no.
    18. Obi nnyi ne mba a ɔawo hɔn nyinara mu a ogya no kwan; eso obi nnyi mba a ɔatsetse hɔn nyinara mu a osuo ne nsamu.
    19. Ndzɛmba ebien yi na aba wo do; woana begyam wo? Amamfo na ɔsɛɛ, nye ɔkɔm na afona; minsi dɛn menkyekye wo werɛ?
    20. Wo mbabanyin atotɔ bitsi, wɔdeda abrɔn nyinara do, dɛ adoa a ɔda efir mu; EWURADZE n'ebufuhyew, wo Nyankopɔn no ntwuwenyim ayeyɛ amaama.
    21. Dɛm ntsi afei tsie iyi, ɔwo ɔmandzehunyi a abow, naaso nnyɛ nsa bi a;
    22. mbrɛ w'EWURADZE, na wo Nyankopɔn a odzi ma ne man no, ɔse nye yi, Hwɛ, magye ntentan kɔɔpow no, mekyerɛ m'ebufuhyew kuraba no efi wo nsamu; erennda ho nnom ara bio:
    23. na medze bɛhyɛ hɔn a wohiahia wo ho no hɔn nsamu; hɔn a wɔase wo kra dɛ, Bɔ wo mu adze, ma yendua do: na ɔwo na edze w'ekyir ato hɔ dɛ famu, na dɛ ɔbrɔn ama hɔn a wodua do no.

    Tsir 52

    1. Nyan ɛ, Ao Zion, nyan ɛ, fa w'ahoɔdzen hyɛ; Ao Jerusalɛm, kurow krɔnkrɔn, fa wo ntar fɛɛfɛw hyɛ: na ofitsi ndɛ dze kɔ yi, monomonomfo na ahoɔfifo nnkɛhɛn wo mu bio., #Nyi 21.2
    2. Popo woho huntuma gu; Jerusalɛm, soɛr ɛ, tsena ase: Zion babaa ndɔmmum, sansan wo kɔn mu nkyehoma no.
    3. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Wɔtɔɔn hom kwa; na wɔnndze sika na wɔdze bɔpon hom.
    4. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE Nyankopɔn se nye yi, Me man sianee kɔr Egypt asɔpɔn no kɛyɛɛ anana wɔ hɔ: na Asirianyi no hyɛɛ hɔn do kwa.
    5. Dɛm ntsi afei, mereyɛ ha bɛn, EWURADZE na ɔse, ber a wɔdze me man kɔ kwa yi? Hɔn a wodzi hɔn do tum no tseatsea mu, EWURADZE na ɔse, na wɔka me dzin ho ebususɛm daa nyina.
    6. Dɛm ntsi me man bohu me dzin: dɛm ntsi da no mu wobohu dɛ emi mara nye nyia ɔkasa; hwɛ, emi nye yi.
    7. Nyia ɔdze nsɛmpa ba no n'anan mbrɛ odua yɛ fɛw wɔ mbepɔw do a, nyia ɔdze asomdwee tahye, nyia ɔdze papa ho nsɛmpa ba, nyia ɔdze nkwagye tahye; nyia ɔse Zion dɛ, Wo Nyame dzi hen!
    8. Tsie! W'aweɔmfo ndze nye no! Wɔma ndze do, wɔbɔ mu tow ndwom; osiandɛ hɔn enyiwa tua EWURADZE, dɛ ɔresan aba Zion.
    9. Jerusalɛm amamfo e, hom ntsew ntɔ enyigye mu, hom mbɔ mu ntow ndwom; na EWURADZE akyekye ne man hɔn werɛ, ɔapon Jerusalɛm.
    10. EWURADZE eyi ne basa krɔnkrɔn no ho wɔ amanaman nyinara enyim; na asaase ewiei nyinara bohu hɛn Nyankopɔn no nkwagye.
    11. Hom ntwe homho, hom ntwe homho, hom mfi hɔ nkɔ, mma hom nka efifidze biara; hom mfi no mu nkɔ; hom ho ntsew, hom a hom soso EWURADZE no nkɔɔpow.
    12. Na hom rimmfi hɔ nnkɔ ɔhardo, na hom nnkotu enguan akɔ bi: EWURADZE bedzi hom enyim; na Israel Nyankopɔn abɔ hom nkyidɔm.
    13. Hwɛ, obesi m'akowaa yie, wobohuhor no na wɔama no do, na ɔakrɔn kɛsekɛse.
    14. Dɛ mbrɛ dodowara hɔn ho dwuruuw hɔn wɔ no ho no, osiandɛ n'enyim sɛɛe seen nyimpa biara, na ne nyimpa su seen adasamba ntsi, ISA.52.15, dɛmara na ɔbɛma amanaman pii abɔ piriw; ahemfo bɛka hɔn ano ato mu wɔ no ho: na dza wɔnnkaa nnkyerɛɛ hɔn pɛn no na wobohu; na dza wɔnntsee pɛn no na wɔbɛtse ase.

    Tsir 53

    1. Woana na ɔagye hɛn amandzɛɛ edzi? Na woana na woeyi EWURADZE ne basa akyerɛ no?
    2. Na onyiin dɛ dua fɔr wɔ n'enyim, na dɛ ndwow a ofi asaase mu: onnyi frɔdɔɔ anaa enyimnyam ɔbɛma yaahwɛ no; onnyi ahoɔfɛw a ɔbɛma no ho ayɛ akɔndɔ.
    3. Adasa buu no enyimtsia, na wɔpoow no; awerɛhow nyimpa a ɔyaw abra no: na dɛ obi a adasa dze hɔn enyim huntsa no, wobuu no enyimtsia, na yeemmbu no hwee.
    4. Ampaara ɔasɔw hɛn yaw, na ɔasoa hɛn awerɛhow: naaso yebuu no dɛ nyia wɔahwe no, Nyankopɔn abɔ no, na woehiahia no ho.
    5. Na mbom wopiraa no wɔ hɛn mbrato ntsi, woposoow no wɔ hɛn emumuyɛ ntsi; wɔdze hɛn asomdwee ho ntsea too no do; na ne mbaa ano na wɔdze asa hɛn yarba.
    6. Hɛn nyinara yɛatotɔ dɔnsuar dɛ nguan; yɛamanman obiara afa noara no kwan do; na EWURADZE dze hɛn nyinara hɛn emumuyɛ ato no do.
    7. Wɔhyɛɛ no do, ɔtsee yaw, naaso ɔbrɛɛ noho adze, na oemmbue n'ano; dɛ eguambaa a wɔdze no rokɔ ekumii, na dɛ oguan a ɔatɔ mmum wɔ no nhwitwitwafo enyim; nyew, oemmbue n'ano., #Nyi 5.6#Ndwu 8.32
    8. Nhyɛdo na atsɛmbu mu na wɔfaa no kɔree; na n'etsipɛmfo dze, hɔn mu woana na ɔdwen dɛ woetwa no efi atseasefo asaase do, na mo nkorɔfo hɔn mbrato ntsi na wɔhwee no?
    9. Wɔbɔɔ ne nda wɔ emumuyɛfo nkyɛn, na ahonyafo nkyɛn wɔ no wu mu; naaso na oenndzi akatabansɛm biara, eso woennhu ndaadaa bi wɔ n'anomu.
    10. Naaso nna ɔyɛ EWURADZE ne pɛ dɛ ɔhyɛ no amen; ɔahyɛ no ɔyaw: ber a ɔdze ne kra bɛyɛ bɔn ho afɔrbɔdze no, obohu n'asefo, ɔbɛma ne nda awar, na EWURADZE ne pɛ bɛyɛ prɔmprɔm wɔ ne nsamu.
    11. Obohu ne kra n'awokodzi, na ɔamee: ɔnam ne nyimdzee do na m'akowaa tseneneenyi bobu piinara bem: na ɔbɔsoa hɔn emumuyɛ.
    12. Dɛm ntsi mebɛkyɛ adze ama ɔno ɔnye akɛsefo, na ɔnye ahoɔdzenfo bɛkyɛ asadze; osiandɛ ohuee ne kra maa owu, na wɔkaan no foraa mbratofo: naaso ɔsoaa dodowara hɔn bɔn, na odzii maa mbratofo.

    Tsir 54

    1. Tow ndwom, ao Ɔbɔnyin, ɔwo a annwo; ɔwo a ennkyeem ɔba da, fa ehurusi ndwom, na tsea mu: na ankonam no ne mba bɔdɔɔ so asen ɔbaa ɔwarfo no ne mba, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    2. Tserɛw wo ntamadan bea no mu, na tserɛtserɛw wo tsenabea ho nkataho tam no mu; mma nnkam do: twetwe wo ntampehoma no mu, na tsintsim wo bɔfondua no.
    3. Na ebɛtserɛw akɔ enyimfa na abankum; na w'asefo bɛfa amanaman no ayɛ hɔndze, na wɔama wɔatsenatsena ekurofo no do.
    4. Mma nnsuro; na w'enyi ronnto; eso mma w'enyim nngu ase; na wɔrennhyɛ wo enyito: na wo werɛ befir wo mbofraber mu enyito, na ennkɛkaa w'ekunayɛ mu adapaabɔ ara bio.
    5. Na wo Bɔfo nye wo kun; ne dzin dze dɔm EWURADZE: na Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no nye wo pomfo: wɔbɛfrɛ no asaase nyinara Nyankopɔn.
    6. Na EWURADZE afrɛ wo dɛ ɔyer a wɔapow no na ɔyaw ekitsa no wɔ sunsum mu, mekyerɛ mbofrabermu yer, aber a wɔatow no akyen, wo Nyankopɔn na ɔse.
    7. Mber tsiabaa bi na madan wo egya; na ehumbɔbɔr kɛse na medze bɔboa w'ano.
    8. Ebufuw mbordo mu na medze m'enyim huntsaa wo kakra; na ɔdomankoma ayamuyie na medze mubohu wo mbɔbɔr, wo pomfo EWURADZE na ɔse.
    9. Na iyi yɛ me dɛ Noa esu no; na dɛ mbrɛ maka ntam dɛ Noa esu no remmpram asaase do bio no, dɛmara so na maka ntam dɛ mo bo nnkofuw wo, eso merennka w'enyim.
    10. Na mbepɔw botutu akɔ, na akoko atwetwe hɔnho; naaso modɔ a otsim dze, orunntutu mmfi wo nkyɛn, eso m'asomdwee ahyɛmudzi no ronntwe noho, EWURADZE a ohu wo mbɔbɔr no na ɔse.
    11. Ao ɔwo amandzehunyi a ehum etu wo, na wɔnnkyekyee wo werɛ, hwɛ, medze w'abo mibesisi wo ntɔnka dubir mu, na medze hoabo atow wo fapem.
    12. Na medze bɔgya abo ayɛ w'abantsifi, na medze epopobibirbo ayɛ w'aponkɛse, na abo fɛɛfɛw a ɔsom bo ayɛ wo kurotsia nyina.
    13. Na wo mba nyinara EWURADZE bɛkyerɛkyerɛ hɔn; na wo mba hɔn asomdwee bɔdɔɔ so.
    14. Ndzeyɛtsenenee mu na wobetsim wo: enye nhyɛdo ntamu bɔtwe, osiandɛ innkosuro; enye ehuyi ntamu twe, osiandɛ ɔnnkɛbɛn wo.
    15. Sɛ, obi huenyan basabasayɛ a, ɔnnam mo do: obiara a obohuenyan basabasayɛ etsia wo no, ɔbɔhwe ase wɔ wo ntsi.
    16. Hwɛ, emi na mabɔ ɔtomfo a ohutsa ogyabiriw mu, na ɔbɔ akodze pue; na emi mara so na mabɔ ɔsɛɛfo dɛ ɔnsɛɛ no.
    17. Akodze biara a wɔbɔ tsia wo no, ɔrennyɛ yie: na tɛkyerɛma biara a ɔbɔsoɛr etsia wo wɔ atsɛmbu mu no, ibobu no fɔ. Iyi nye EWURADZE no nkowaa hɔn egyapadze, na hɔn tsenenee a ofi emi mara, EWURADZE na ɔse.

    Tsir 55

    1. Ao, obiara a nsukɔm dze no no, hom mbra esu no ho, na nyia onnyi sika; hom mbra mbɔtɔ, na hom ndzi. Nyew, hom mbra mbɔtɔ wenyin na numfonsu a wɔnndze sika na wonntwa bo so.
    2. Ebɛnadze ntsi na hom hwer sika ma dza ɔnnyɛ edziban, na hom berɛ ma dza ɔmmee? Hom nyɛ aso mma me yie, na hom ndzi dza oye, na hom mma angoanam nyɛ hom kra dɛw.
    3. Hom nkyɛn hom aso, na hom mbra me nkyɛn; hom ntsie, na hom akra bɛtsena ase: na menye hom bedzi ɔdomankoma ahyɛmu. David n'ehumbɔbɔr a osi pi no a.
    4. Hwɛ, medze no ama dɛ aman hɔn dasefo, aman hɔn kwankyerɛfo na ɔsafohen.
    5. Hwɛ, ebɛfrɛ ɔman a innyim hɔn, na ɔman a wonnyim wo no, wɔdze mbirika bɛba wo nkyɛn, osian EWURADZE Nyankopɔn, na Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no ntsi; na ɔno na ɔahyɛ wo enyimnyam.
    6. Hom nhwehwɛ EWURADZE ber a wobohu no yi, hom mfrɛ no ber a ɔbɛn yi:
    7. hom mma omumuyɛnyi ndan no kwan ngya, na ɔbrakyewnyi ndan n'adwen ngya: na ɔnsan mbra EWURADZE nkyɛn, na obohu no mbɔbɔr; na hɛn Nyankopɔn nkyɛn, na ɔdze bɛkyɛ mbordo.
    8. Na nnyɛ m'adwen nye hom adwen, eso nnyɛ hom akwan nye m'akwan, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    9. Na dɛ mbrɛ ɔsorsor krɔn bɔ asaase do no, dɛmara na m'akwan krɔn bɔ hom akwan do, na m'adwen bɔ hom adwen do.
    10. Na dɛ mbrɛ nsu na esukwankyɛba fi sor gu famu, na ɔnnsan hɔ bio, na mbom ɔfɔw asaase, na ɔma ofifir aba na ɔbɔ nhyiren, na ɔdze aba ma oduafo, na edziban ma edzifo no;
    11. mbrɛ asɛm a ofi m'anomu fir no ɔbɛyɛ ara nye no: ɔrennsan mmba mo hɔ kwa, gyedɛ oewie dza mepɛ yɛ, na ɔayɛ prɔmprɔm wɔ dza osian ntsi ma mosomaa no no mu.
    12. Na hom dze enyigye befir akɔ, na wɔdze asomdwee egya hom kwan: mbepɔw na akoko bɛfa ehurusi ndwom edzi hom enyim, na hamu ndua nyinara abobɔ hɔn nsamu.
    13. Pepeaa befir nsoɛ ananmu, na ohuam dua efir kɔkrɔw ananmu: na ɔbɛyɛ nkaa dzin ama EWURADZE, na daa asɛnkyerɛdze a worunntwa nnkyen.

    Tsir 56

    1. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi; Hom nyɛ pɛrpɛr, na hom nyɛ ndzeyɛtsenenee: na mo nkwagye abɛn, ɔreba, na woribeyi me tsenenee akyerɛ.
    2. Osiarfo nye nyimpa a ɔyɛ iyi, na nyimpa ba a osuo mu dzen; nyia osie ahomgyeda no dɛ onngu ho fi, na osie ne nsa fi mbusu biara no bɔ ho.
    3. Mma ɔhɔho a ɔdze noho abɔbɔ EWURADZE ho no, nnka dɛ, Ɔtsew ara na EWURADZE bɛtsew me efi ne man ho: eso mma ɔsaa nnse dɛ, Hwɛ, emi dze meyɛ dua wui.
    4. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se wɔ asaa no a wosie m'ahomgyenda, na wɔsan mu yi ndzɛmba a ɔsɔ m'enyi, na wosuo m'ahyɛmudzi mu pintsinn no ho nye yi:
    5. hɔn na medze me fie na m'afasu mu nkaadze ɔnye dzin a oye sen mbabanyin na mbabaa bɛma; mebɛma hɔn ɔdomankoma dzin a worunntwa nnkyen.
    6. Nkyii so ananaben a wɔdze hɔnho bɔ EWURADZE ho, dɛ wɔrosom no, na wɔadɔ EWURADZE ne dzin dɛ wɔbɛyɛ no nkowaa no, obiara a osie ahomgyeda a onngu ho fi, na osuo m'ahyɛmudzi mu pintsinn no;
    7. hɔnara so mpo na medze hɔn bɛba me bepɔw krɔnkrɔn no do, na mama hɔn enyi agye wɔ m'asɔrfi no mu; hɔn hyew afɔr na hɔn kum afɔr bɛyɛ enyisɔ wɔ m'afɔrmbukyia no do: na wɔbɛfrɛ me fie mpaabɔ ama aman nyinara.
    8. EWURADZE Nyankopɔn a ɔboaboa Israel atokyemfo no ano no, ɔse dɛ, Mebɛda ho ara maboa binom so ano abrɛ no, aka nankasa ne dza wɔaboa ano no ho.
    9. Hom hambowa nyinara, nyew, hom kwaa mu mbowadoma nyinara, hom mbra mbɛmemen.
    10. N'aweɔmfo enyi efurafura, hɔn nyinara wonnyim dze; hɔn nyinara akraman mmum a, wonntum mmpuow; wɔsoso adaa, wɔdeda hɔ, wɔpɛ nkontɔ.
    11. Nyew, akraman no etumfur a, wɔremmee da; na woyinom nye nguanhwɛfo a wonntum nntse adze ase: hɔn nyinara amanaman afa hɔnankasa hɔn kwan do, obiara rohwehwɛ ne mfaso wɔ kwan biara do.
    12. Wɔse dɛ, Hom mbra, medze nsa bɛba ma yɛawe nsadzen; na ɔkyena bɛyɛ dɛ ndɛ, da kɛse a ɔdɔɔ so mbordo.

    Tsir 57

    1. Ɔtseneneenyi hera, naaso obiara mmfa nnto n'akoma mu; wɔfa Nyamesuronyi kɔ, ber a obiara nntse ase. Mbusu a ɔreba no ho na woeyi ɔtseneneenyi efi, ISA.57.2, ɔkɛhɛn asomdwee mu; wɔhom wɔ hɔn mpa do, obiara a ɔnantsew no tɔɔtsenyɛ mu no.
    2. Na hom ɔbayifo ne mbabanyin, awartonyi na edwaman asefo, hom ntwe mbɛn ha.
    3. Woana na hom kyerɛ hom ho wɔ no do yi? Woana na hom hanhan hom anomu, na hom worɔworɔw tɛkyerɛma wɔ no do yi? Aso hom nnyɛ mbrato mba, akɔhwi asefo, ISA.57.5, hom a hom bɔ hom ho hyew wɔ nsudur mu, wɔ dua ebun ebun ase; hom a hom kuku mboframba wɔ mbɔnsa no mu, wɔ abotan no ne mpaapaae no ase?
    4. Mbɔnsa no mu abo tortor no mu na wo kyɛfa wɔ; hɔn, hɔnara nye w'afamudze: hɔnara mpo so na ehue ehuensa egu hɔn do, na abɔ hɔn edziban afɔr. Aso mo bo bɔdwe wɔ iyinom ho?
    5. Bepɔw sorɔnsorɔm a ɔkrɔn etsifi na akɔtow wo kɛtɛ: hɔ ara so na efowee kɔree kɔbɔɔ okum afɔr.
    6. Na mbobow na apondua ekyir na edze wo nkaadze esi: na apa m'ekyir, eyi woho akyerɛ obi so, na afow kɔ; ɔwo atserɛw wo kɛtɛ mu, na enye hɔn edzi ahyɛmu; epɛɛ hɔn kɛtɛ no wɔ mbrɛ ihunii no.
    7. Na edze seradze sii mu kɔr ɔhen ne nkyɛn, na emaa w'eduhuam dɔɔ so, na esomaa w'ahembɔfo ekyirekyir, na etoo woho adze ara kɔr samanadze mpo.
    8. Wo kwan ne tsentsen maa eberɛe; naaso annka dɛ, Enyidado nnyi hɔ: inyaa w'ahoɔdzen no nkwa; dɛm ntsi na anntɔ bitsi.
    9. Na woana na w'akoma etu no ho na esuro no, ma idzi ator, na annkaa me, eso anndwen mo ho yi? Ana ommfir tsetse na maka m'ano ato mu komm, na ɔwo innsuro me yi?
    10. Mebɛka wo tsenenee na wo ndwuma akyerɛ; naaso ɔrennyɛ wo mfaso bi.
    11. Sɛ etsea mu a, ma w'abosom a aprapra hɔn aboa ano no wɔngye wo; na mframa bɛfa hɔn akɔ, ehuw bɔsoa hɔn nyinara akɔ: na nyia ɔdze no werɛ twer me no, obenya asaase no edzi, na oenya me bepɔw krɔnkrɔn no atsena do.
    12. Na ɔbɛka dɛ, Hom nhyehyɛ, hom nhyehyɛ, hom nsiesie kwan no, hom nyiyi mfintsidua no wɔ me man hɔn kwan mu.
    13. Na mbrɛ nyia ɔkrɔn na ɔyɛ abɔso a ɔtse onnyiewiei mu, na ne dzin nye Krɔnkrɔn no ɔse nye yi: Metse bea a ɔkrɔn na ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn do, wɔ nyia no sunsum abobɔ na abrɛ adze nkyɛn so, dɛ mebɛhyɛ ahobrɛadzefo sunsum nkwa, na mahwɛ hɔn a hɔn akoma abobɔ nkwa.
    14. Na mirinndzi esi ara afebɔɔ, eso mo bo rummfuw daa: nkyɛ sunsum na akra a mara mayɛ no, wɔtɔ bahaw wɔ m'enyim.
    15. N'enyiber emumuyɛ ntsi na mo bo fuwii na mobɔɔ no, muhuntsaa m'enyim na mo bo fuwii: naaso ɔdaa ho ara nantseew akɔnkyew mu wɔ n'akoma no kwan mu.
    16. Mehu ne ndzeyɛɛ, naaso mebɛsa no yarba: mibegya no kwan so, na madan awerɛkyekyer ama no, na medze nsɛm a ɔyɛ dɛw ahyɛ no nkɔmbɔdzifo ano.
    17. Asomdwee, asomdwee, nka nyia ɔwɔ ekyirekyir na nyia ɔbɛn, EWURADZE na ɔse; na mebɛsa no yarba.
    18. Naaso emumuyɛfo tse dɛ po a ɔapram; osiandɛ ɔda a ɔnnda, na n'esu puw dɛtsebir na nwura gu.
    19. Asomdwee bi nnyi hɔ ma emumuyɛfo, me Nyankopɔn na ɔse.

    Tsir 58

    1. Tsea mu, mma nnkam do, ma wo ndze do dɛ akasamu, na ka me man hɔn mbrato kyerɛ hɔn, na ka Jakob fifo hɔn bɔn kyerɛ hɔn.
    2. Naaso wɔhwehwɛ me daa daa, na wɔpɛ dɛ wohu m'akwan: dɛ gyama ɔman bi a wɔyɛɛ ndzeyɛtsenenee, na wɔanndan hɔn Nyankopɔn nhyehyɛɛ enngya, wobisa mo hɔ atsɛntsenenee, wɔpɛ dɛ wopinkyɛn Nyankopɔn.
    3. Ebɛnadze ntsi na yeedzi mbuada, na ɔwo innhu? Yeehiahia hɛn kra ho, na ɔwo mmfa nnyɛ hwee yi? Hwɛ, hom mbuadadzi da no mu, hom nya homankasa hom enyigye, na hom tseetsee hom edwumayɛfo.
    4. Hwɛ, mansotwe na etutuwpɛ ntsi na hom dzi mbuada, na hom awowɔ emumuyɛ ekutuku: nnyɛ hom ndɛ mbuadadzi yi na ɔbɛma wɔaatse hom ndze wɔ sor.
    5. Aso iyi nye mbuada a masan mu meyi no? Aso da a nyimpa hiahia ne kra ho nye yi? Aso ɔno nye dɛ ɔbɔbɔ ne tsir adze dɛ mbɛw, na ɔdze eyitam na nso asɛw n'ananadze? Aso ebɛfrɛ iyi dɛ mbuadadzi, na da a ɔsɔ EWURADZE enyi?
    6. Ana nnyɛ iyi nye mbuadadzi a masan mu meyi? Dɛ hom bɛsansan emumuyɛ apɔw no, wɔapopɔr kɔndua nhoma no, na wɔama hɔn a wɔatseetsee hɔn no wɔaafa hɔnho edzi akɔ, na hom eebubu kɔndua nyina mu?
    7. Ana nnyɛ ɔno nye dɛ ibubu w'edziban ma nyia ɔkɔm dze no, na dɛ edze abɔbɔfo a woeyi hɔn tokyen no ba wo fie? Sɛ ihu ɔdagyanyi a, ekata no ho; na dɛ emmfa woho nnhuntsa woara wo busuanyi.
    8. Ɔno na wo kan bɛgyegye dɛ adzekyee, na w'ayarsa efifir ntsɛm: na wo tsenenee bedzi w'enyim; EWURADZE n'enyimnyam bɔbɔ wo nkyidɔm.
    9. Ɔno na ebɛfrɛ, na EWURADZE bɛgye do; ebɛtsea mu, na ɔbɛse dɛ, Emi nye yi oo. Sɛ iyi kɔndua no, nsatseaba ne tsen, na ehuhukasa fi wo mu;
    10. na sɛ edze dza wo kra no kɔn dɔ ma nyia ɔkɔm dze no, na ma ɔkra a oruhu amandze mee a; nna wo kan bopue wɔ sum mu, na wo kusuww ayɛ dɛ ewiaber ketee:
    11. na EWURADZE begya wo kwan daa, na ɔama wo kra amee wɔ mbrɛ hɔ yɛ kwawee, na ɔama wo mbiew ayɛ dzen; na ebɛyɛ dɛ ture a woegugu mu nsu, na dɛ mbasu a no nsu nntwe.
    12. Na hɔn a wobefi wo mu no bɛkyekyer tsetse ekurofo no: na wɔbɛfrɛ wo Osiw etu, Nyia ɔsesɛw akwan a wɔtsena mu.
    13. Sɛ iyi w'anan fi ahomgyeda no ho, na annyɛ wo pɛ ho edwuma wɔ me da krɔnkrɔn no mu; na efrɛ ahomgyeda no enyigyedze, na EWURADZE n'akrɔnkrɔndze no dɛ enyimnyamdze; na idzi no nyi, na annyɛ woara wo kwan do adze, na annhwehwɛ woara w'enyigye, na annka woara wo nsɛm a:
    14. ɔno na ebɛgye w'enyi wɔ EWURADZE mu; na mama anantsew asaase nsorɔnsorɔmbea do; na mama edzi w'egya Jakob n'egyapadze: na EWURADZE ano na ɔaka.

    Tsir 59

    1. Hwɛ, EWURADZE ne basa nntwaa tsia, dɛ onntum nkwa gye; eso n'asomu nnyɛ dzen, dɛ ɔnntse asɛm:
    2. na mbom hom emumuyɛ na apaa hom nye hom Nyankopɔn ntamu, na hom bɔn na oehuntsa n'enyi efi hom do, ma onnketsie.
    3. Na bɔgya egu hom nsa ho fi, na emumuyɛ ehura hom nsatseaba ho; hom anofamfa aka atorsɛm, hom tɛkyerɛma hwinhwin ehuhusɛm.
    4. Obiara nnsaman tsenenee mu, na obiara nndzi n'asɛm wɔ nokwar mu: wɔdze hɔn werɛ hyɛ egyangyandze mu, na wɔka atorsɛm; wonyinsen ewurkadze, na wɔwo emumuyɛ.
    5. Wosuow akyerben nkyirefuwa, na wɔwen ananse ntentan: nyia odzi hɔn nkyirefuwa bi no, owu, na dza wɔbobɔ no, ɔpaa ehurutsia.
    6. Hɔn ntentan no renndan atar, eso wɔremmfa hɔn ndwuma nnkata hɔnho: hɔn ndwuma yɛ emumuyɛ ndwuma, na akakabensɛm wɔ hɔn nsamu.
    7. Hɔn anan tutu mbirika kɔ mbusu mu, na wɔyɛ ntsɛm kɛka nyia onndzi fɔ no bɔgyaa gu: hɔn adwen yɛ emumuyɛ adwen; amamfoyɛ na ɔsɛɛ wɔ akwan mu.
    8. Asomdwee ɔtsempɔn no dze wonnyim; na atsɛmbu biara nnyi hɔn nkɔree mu: wɔabɔ hɔn akwan akyewakyew; obiara a ɔfa mu no onnyim asomdwee.
    9. Dɛm ntsi na atsɛmbu nye hɛn ntamu atwe, eso ndzeyɛtsenenee nnto hɛn: yɛhwɛ kan kwan, na hwɛ, sum nye yi; ɔhyerɛn so, na mbom yɛnam sunkamm mu.
    10. Yɛkeka ban ho dɛ ofurafo, nyew, yɛkeka dɛ hɔn a wonnyi enyiwa: yefintsiw ewiaber ketee dɛ wantawanta ber mu; yɛayɛ dɛ ewufo wɔ hɔn a wɔyɛ atwɛntwɛmfo mu.
    11. Hɛn nyinara yɛpopɔw dɛ nsisi, na yɛka mmɔn pii dɛ mbubur: yɛhwɛ atsɛmbu kwan, naaso bi nnyi hɔ; nkwagye so, na ɔnye hɛn ntamu atwe koraa.
    12. Na hɛn mbrato adɔɔ so pii wɔ w'enyim, na hɛn bɔn gye dase tsia hɛn: osiandɛ hɛn mbrato wɔ hɛn nkyɛn, na hɛn emumuyɛ dze, yenyim:
    13. wɔ mbrato na EWURADZE do nkontompɔtwa mu, na ɔsan a yɛasan efi hɛn Nyankopɔn n'ekyirdzi mu, nhyɛdo na etuatsew ne ka, atorsɛm a yɛadwendwen ho na yeefi akoma mu aka.
    14. Na wɔadan atsɛmbu asan ekyir, na ndzeyɛtsenenee ekegyina ekyirekyir noho: osiandɛ nokwar ahwe ase wɔ abɔntsen do, na tɔɔtsenyɛ nntum nnhɛn mu.
    15. Nyew, nokwar asa; na nyia otwa noho fi mbusu ho no, ɔyɛ noho afonam: na EWURADZE hunii, na ɔannyɛ no abodwe dɛ atsɛmbu bi nnyi hɔ.
    16. Na ohun dɛ nyimpa biara nnyi hɔ, na ɔyɛɛ no nwanwa dɛ odzimafo bi nnyi hɔ: dɛm ntsi nankasa ne basa na ɔdze nkwagye brɛɛ no; na ne ndzeyɛtsenenee no, osuoo no mu gyinae.
    17. Na ɔdze ndzeyɛtsenenee hyɛɛ dɛ akatabo, na nkwagye kyɛw so ne tsir; na ɔhyɛɛ awerdzi ntar dɛ akataho, na ɔhyɛɛ mbɔdzembɔ dɛ atar egugudo., #Efe 6.14
    18. Mbrɛ hɔn ndzeyɛɛ tse no, dɛmara na ɔbɛhyɛ hɔn ananmu, ɔdze ebufuhyew ama n'ahohiahiafo, akatua a ɔsɛ ama n'atamfo; nsuano aman no so ɔdze akatua a ɔfata bɛma hɔn.
    19. Dɛm no bɛma wofi anee esuro EWURADZE ne dzin, na wofi wipuei esuro n'enyimnyam: na ɔbɛba dɛ esutsen a ɔrepem yaayaa a EWURADZE n'ehum ripia no.
    20. Na ɔpomfo bɛba Zion, na hɔn a wɔsan fi mbrato ho wɔ Jakob mu no nkyɛn, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    21. Na emi dze, menye hɔn ntamu ahyɛmu no nye yi, EWURADZE na ɔse: mo sunsum a ɔwɔ wo do, na me nsɛm a medze mahyɛ w'ano no rimmfi w'anomu, anaa w'asefo hɔn asefo so anomu, ofitsi ndɛ dze kesi daa, EWURADZE na ɔse.

    Tsir 60

    1. Soɛr, hyerɛn; na wo kan aba, na EWURADZE n'enyimnyam asoɛr wo do.
    2. Na, hwɛ, sum bɛkata asaase do, na sum kebii akata aman do: na EWURADZE befir wo do, na n'enyimnyam woehu no wo do.
    3. Na amanaman bɛba wo kan ho, na ahemfo aba wo mfirii ne hyerɛn ho.
    4. Ma w'enyi do bɔ aprɔw, na hwɛ; hɔn nyinara wɔboa hɔn ano, wɔba wo nkyɛn: wo mbabanyin fi ekyirekyir bɛba, na wo mbabaa so woetutur hɔn abaw mu.
    5. Ɔno na ibohu na w'enyim atsew, na w'akoma behihim na ɔayɛ kɛse; osiandɛ po mu ndzepa bɛdan aba wo hɔ, amanaman ahonya bɛba wo hɔ.
    6. Efumpɔnkɔ menyamenya bɛkata wo do, Midian na Efa efumpɔnkɔfɔr; hɔn nyinara wofi Seba bɛba. Wɔdze sika na nduhuam, na wɔbɔbɔ EWURADZE n'ayɛyi dawur.
    7. Kedar mbowa ekuwekuw nyina bɔboa ano aba wo nkyɛn, Nebaiot nguannyin bɔsom wo; wɔbɔfow aba m'afɔrmbukyia no do enyisɔ mu, na mahyɛ m'enyimnyam fi no enyimnyam.
    8. Woananom nye woyi a wotu dɛ nsuwusiw, na dɛ mbubur a wɔrokɔ hɔn ntokura mu yi?
    9. Ampaara nsuano aman bɔtweɔn me, na Tarsis ahɛn dzi kan, dɛ wɔdze wo mbabanyin fi ekyirekyir reba, hɔn dwetɛ na hɔn sika ka hɔn ho, wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne dzin ntsi, na Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no ntsi, osiandɛ ɔno na ɔahyɛ wo enyimnyam.
    10. Na ananaben bɔtow w'afasu, na hɔn ahemfo bɔsom wo: na m'ebufuw mu na mobɔɔ wo, na m'enyimpa mu na mehu wo mbɔbɔr.
    11. W'aponkɛse so bɛda hɔ daa; wɔronntotow mu adzekyee na adzesaa; ama adasa wɔdze amanaman ahonya aabrɛ wo, na wɔaaka hɔn ahemfo aka hɔn ho aba.
    12. Na ɔman na ahenman biara a ɔnnkɔsom wo no, ɔbɛhera; nyew, amanaman no bɔbɔ huntuhuntu.
    13. Lebanon n'enyimnyam bɛba wo hɔ, ɔpepeaa, ɔsɛsɛw, na ɔpapaa dua bɔbɔ mu, dze abɛyɛ mo krɔnkrɔnbea hɔ fɛɛfɛw, na maahyɛ m'anan tsiabea no enyimnyam.
    14. Na hɔn a wohiahiaa wo ho no hɔn mbabanyin dze akotokotow bɛba wo nkyɛn; na hɔn a wobuu wo enyimtsia nyinara dze hɔn enyim bobom w'ananadze; na wɔbɛfrɛ wo EWURADZE no kuropɔn, Israel Krɔnkrɔnnyi no ne Zion.
    15. Susuampaara dɛ wɔadan wo egya na woekyir wo, na nyimpa biara ammfa wo mu ntsi, mebɛyɛ wo otsitsir daa, na mayɛ mbasantsen pii hɔn enyigye.
    16. Eso ebɔnom amanaman numfonsu, na enum ahemfo hɔn enumfo: na ibohu dɛ emi EWURADZE nye w'agyenkwa, na wo pomfo, Jakob ne Katakyi no.
